It had an authentic flavour, and the [[Meat|meat]] turned out incredibly tender thanks to the extended cooking time achieved by using a [[Pressure cooker|pressure cooker]].\n\nThis is now a regular staple, together with [[How long to cook Oakhurst Aldi Peri Peri Chicken King Kebab|Aldi's Peri-Peri King Kebab]].  We now make this, eat half and freeze the remainder for another meal together. \n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 jar of Aldi's Fiesta [[Chilli con carne|chilli con carne]] (Hot)\n| 1 kg of [[Stewing steak|stewing steak]]; ours is from [[Russell's Butchers of Upwell, Norfolk]]\n| 1 400g can [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]]\n| 1 340g can [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]]\n| &#189; teaspoon very [[Hot chilli powder|hot chilli powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Taste Sensation fajita seasoning]] mix\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Drain the [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]] and rinse well\n| Drain and rinse the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]]\n| Cut the [[Steak|steak]] into fairly small pieces as they tend to be on the large size\n| Pour the Fiesta [[Chilli con carne|chilli con carne]] [[Sauce|sauce]] into a large bowl that will fit into your [[Pressure cooker|pressure cooker]]\n| Rinse the jar with a little water or [[Sherry|sherry]] if you're feeling lush!\n| Add the remaining ingredients and mix well\n| Pressure cook on heigh for 2 hours (would be done in 1 hour, but 2 makes the meat super tender)\n| Allow to de-pressurise naturally\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Aldis Fiesta Chilli Con Carne with Cubed Steak ingredients.jpg|All of the ingredients\nImage:Aldis Fiesta Chilli Con Carne with Cubed Steak mixed and ready to cook.jpg|Mixed well and ready to pressure cook\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nWe had this over two days; firstly with [[Taco shells|taco shells]] and then I had mine with [[Curly fries|curly fries]] and Anne had her second lot with [[Rice|rice]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThis was a superb [[Chilli|chilli]] with just the right heat.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilean recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pressure cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Pressure cooked]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#pressurecooker #sweetcorn #kidneybeans #aldisfiestachilliconcarnewithcubedsteak #chilliconcarne #rice #chillipepperrecipes #garlicrecipes #steak #beefrecipes #sherry</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Atole",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Atole: Cooking Wiki\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#atole #masa #cornmeal #chocolate #riceflour #fruit #cornstarch #toasted #beverages #piloncillo #vanilla \n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=Atole is a traditional cornstarch-based Mexican and Central American (where it is known as atol) hot drink\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n[[Image:Mas vale atole.jpg|300px|thumb|right|M\u00e1s vale atole con risas, que chocolate con l\u00e1grimas]]\n'''Atole''' is a traditional [[cornstarch]]-based Mexican and Central American (where it is known as atol) hot drink. [[Chocolate]] atole is known as champurrado. It is typically accompanied with [[tamales]], and very popular during the Christmas holiday season (Las Posadas).\n\nThe drink typically includes [[masa]] ([[corn meal]]), water, [[piloncillo]], [[cinnamon]], [[vanilla]] and optional [[chocolate]] or [[fruit]]. The mixture is blended and heated before serving. The resulting blends vary in texture, ranging from a porridge to a very thin liquid consistency. Atole can also be prepared with [[rice flour]] or [[oatmeal]] in place of [[masa]]. In northern Mexico there is also a variation using pinole (sweetened toasted corn meal). Although atole is one of the traditional drinks of the Mexican holiday Day of the Dead, it is very common during breakfast and dinnertime at any time of year. It is usually sold as street food.\n\nOther derivations exist. In New Mexico, blue corn atole is finely ground [[cornmeal]] [[toasted]] for cooking, consumed as a grainy porridge-style drink served warm, usually sweetened with [[sugar]] and/or thinned with [[milk]]. It is usually served at breakfast like cream of wheat or oatmeal. It is said that elders would drink Atole because it gave them energy and if a mother is nursing it gives them more [[milk]]. \n\nSalvadoran varieties include atol shuco (\"dirty\" atol, a reference to its darker colour), particularly popular in the Caba\u00f1as region.\n{{CategoryLineIngredients}}\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n[[Category:Beverages]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Non-alcoholic beverages]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#atole #masa #cornmeal #chocolate #riceflour #fruit #cornstarch #toasted #beverages #piloncillo #vanilla </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

teaspoon [[sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[demerara sugar]] or [[jaggery]]\n| 3 teaspoons [[olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[lime juice]], [[chili]], [[salt]], [[sugar]] and [[oil]] together in a bowl\n| Cut some deep slashes into the flesh so the [[marinade]] can 'work' on the meat\n| Marinate the [[chicken]] in a [[refrigerator]] for 2 hours or more, turning a few times\n| [[Barbecue]] the chicken for about 15 minutes on a well oiled grill, turning often to prevent burning\n| Check the [[chicken]] is properly cooked before serving\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with a green salad, [[jacket potatoes]], [[sour cream]] and [[Pickled jalape\u00f1os]]\n===Variations===\nYou could make this with [[chicken thighs]] or [[drumsticks]].  Larger pieces will take a little longer to cook.  Check the juices run clear when the thickest part is pierced with a fork.\n\nThese can also be cooked on an oven tray with a rack at 180\u00b0 C [350\u00b0 F - Gas 4 - Moderate/Medium]. Allow 40 minutes for small pieces like wings. 50 minutes for larger pieces like thighs and drumsticks. Check juices run clear and leave to [[rest]] for 5 minutes before serving.    \nTry this [[marinade]] with [[lamb tenderloin fillets]] or [[king prawns]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Marinaded]][[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #barbecuedlimeandchilichickenwings #chili #limejuice #marinade #grilled #jaggery #refrigerator #rest #barbecued #drumsticks </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It is very quick and easy to produce, making it a balanced, inexpensive meal for students\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2266\n|PortionCalories = 566\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Beef and bean cottage pie recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">An odd idea, but good.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A nice change from rice</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThis is a mixture of [[Chilli con carne]] and [[Cottage pie]].  It is very quick and easy to produce, making it a balanced, inexpensive meal for students\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 medium or 1 large [[Onion|onion]], chopped\n| 300g [[Minced beef|minced beef]]\n| 200g [[Baked beans|baked beans]]\n| 200g [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]], drained\n| 1.5 teaspoons [[Marmite]], [[Vegemite]] or [[Bovril]]\n| 1-2 teaspoons [[Dried mixed herbs|dried mixed herbs]]\n| 1-2 tablespoons dired [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]]\n| 1kg [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled\n| 250g [[Carrots|carrots]], peeled\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, crushed\n| A little [[Milk|milk]] or a knob of [[butter]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] over a high heat and saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] until golden [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the [[Mince|mince]] and cook until [[Brown|brown]].\n| Stir in the [[Baked beans|baked beans]], [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]],  [[Marmite]], [[Vegemite]] or [[Bovril]], the [[Dried mixed herbs|dried mixed herbs]] and the [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]].\n| Transfer to a [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]].\n| Meanwhile, [[Boil|boil]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and the [[Carrots|carrots]] until cooked - about 20 minutes.\n| Drain and [[Mash|mash]] together, adding the [[Milk|milk]] and the [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Season to taste.\n| Spread out the [[Potato|potato]] over the [[Meat|meat]] and [[Bean|bean]] mixture in the [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]] and drag a fork through it to create a pretty pattern.\n| [[Bake]] at 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour] for 20 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Peas|peas]] and / or [[Beans|beans]]\n===Variations===\nIf you don't like [[Chillies|chillies]] or [[Garlic|garlic]], just leave them out.  Use any type of tinned [[Beans|beans]] to replace the [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]].  Substitute the [[Carrot|carrot]] for [[Swede|swede]].  Grate some [[Parmesan]] or other hard [[Cheese|cheese]] over the top of the [[Potato|potato]] / carrot mixture before [[Baking|baking]]\n===See also===\n* {{ChiliConCarne}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pies tarts and flans]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beefandbeancottagepie #kidneybeans #garlic #driedmixedherbs #carrots #bovril #potato #casseroledish #chilliflakes #potatoes #vegemite </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I am becoming very impressed with their products!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 350g [[beef skirt]] (or [[Stewing steak|stewing steak]])\n| 3 tablespoons [[Taste Sensation fajita seasoning]]\n| 1 whole [[Lime|lime]], un-squeezed and sliced into eighths\n| 1 [[Red onion|red onion]], chopped\n| 1 [[Green bell pepper|green bell pepper]], de-seeded and chopped\n| 250 ml [[White wine|white wine]]\n| 200 ml water\n| 1 can of [[Red kidney beans|red kidney beans]], drained and well rinsed\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Marinade]] the [[beef skirt]] in the [[Wine|wine]] for a few hours if you have the time\n| Pop the [[Meat|meat]] in the [[Slow Cooker|slow cooker]] and pour the [[Wine|wine]] over the [[beef skirt|skirt]] and add the water\n| Cover with the remaining ingredients and cook on a high setting for about six hours\n| Check it does not dry out and that the [[Meat|meat]] is tender and starting to break up.\n| Add the [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]] for the final hour\n| Stir well and serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe in warmed [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]] with a [[Salad|salad]] and slices of [[Citrus fruit|citrus fruit]]\n===Variations===\nA whole [[leek]], finely chopped looks good as a replacement for the onion, if leeks are in season.\n\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Beef skirt]] is a fabulous, inexpensive cut for this dish.  It does need a lot of cooking, but once it begins to break up into 'strings' as you can see in the 'plated-up' picture you know it's tender and ready to eat.  At this point you can turn the heat down and just keep the meat warm until you're ready to serve.\n\nI added the [[kidney beans]] to bulk out the meal a little, and also as a way to soak up the gorgeous flavours.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Chilean recipes]]\n[[Category:Ecuadorian recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beefskirt #kidneybeans #beefskirtsteakfajitas #wine #greenbellpepper #tastesensationrecipes #leek #redkidneybeans #lime #whitewine #salad </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Emmenthal cheese]] is obviously not authentic, but I just love it, so [[Emmenthal]] it is.  Use any [[Cheese|cheese]] of your choice.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 pack of [[Flour|flour]] [[Tortillas|tortillas]]\n| 175 g can of [[Black beans|black beans]]\n| 165 g can of [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] kernels\n| 350 g bottle of [[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]]\n| 150 ml tub of [[Sour cream|sour cream]]\n| 200g [[Emmenthal cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 3 fresh or [[Pickled|pickled]] [[Red chillies|red chillies]] (or to taste)\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Tip the [[Salsa|salsa]] into a bowl\n| Chop the [[Chillies|chillies]] finely, remove the [[Seeds|seeds]] if you don't want it too hot.\n| Rinse and drain the [[Black beans|black beans]]\n| Place 2/3rds of the [[Beans|beans]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade and blend to a chunky paste\n| Add the blended [[Beans|beans]] and the remaining whole [[Beans|beans]] to the bowl\n| Add the [[Salsa|salsa]] to the bowl, stir in the [[Chillies|chillies]] and mix well\n| Reserve about 4 tablespoons of the [[Bean|bean]]/[[Salsa|salsa]] mix to a saucer to top the [[Burritos|burritos]]\n| Rinse and drain the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] and add to the bowl of [[Beans|beans]] with 2/3rds of the [[Sour cream|sour cream]] and mix well.  Keep the rest of the [[Cream|cream]] to serve with the [[Burritos|burritos]]\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] a [[Baking|baking]] dish\n| Fill 6 [[Tortillas|tortillas]] with the [[Bean|bean]] mix from the bowl, roll them up and place in the [[Baking|baking]] dish, seam-side down\n| Spread the reserved [[Bean|bean]] mixture from the saucer over the [[Burritos|burritos]] and cover with [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| [[Bake]] for 20 minutes or until heated through.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with the remaining [[Sour cream|sour cream]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Cuban recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beans #sourcream #blackbeanburritos #salsa #burritos #bean #chillies #baking #emmenthalcheese #sweetcorn #cheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Caesar salad",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Caesar salad, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#salad #oliveoil #worcestershiresauce #caesarsalad #anchovies #lettuce #egg #garlic #blackpepper #parmesancheese #croutons \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A typical Caesar salad comprises romaine lettuce and croutons dressed with parmesan cheese, lemon juice, olive oil, egg, Worcestershire sauce, and\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 763\n|PortionCalories = 190\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 as a snack, or 6 as a [[Starter|starter]] / side [[Salad|salad]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 5 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Caesar salad recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wheel out that Hostess Trolley.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This recipe deserves to be served properly! \ud83d\ude01</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nA typical Caesar [[Salad|salad]] comprises romaine [[Lettuce|lettuce]] and [[croutons]] dressed with [[Parmesan cheese|parmesan cheese]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Egg|egg]], [[Worcestershire sauce]], and [[Black pepper|black pepper]] originally prepared tableside. Caesar Cardini (Italian-born [[Mexican]]) is credited with creating the salad.\n\nContrary to popular belief, the original Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] recipe did not contain pieces of [[Anchovy|anchovy]]; the slight anchovy flavour comes from the [[Worcestershire sauce]]. Cardini was opposed to using [[Anchovies|anchovies]] in his salad.\n\nIn the book From Julia Child's Kitchen, Julia Child describes how she ate a Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] at Cardini's restaurant when she was a child in 1920s, and some 50 years later she sought out and called Cardini's daughter, in order to discover the original recipe. In this recipe, [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves are served whole on the plate, because they are meant to be lifted by the stem and eaten with the fingers. It also calls for coddled [[Eggs|eggs]] and Italian [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nRather than re create the absolute original recipe, I have chosen to go for a composite of many current 'favourite' recipes.\n\n\n'''[[Salad]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 small cos [[Lettuce|lettuce]], washed and separated into leaves\n| 1 50 g (2 oz) can of [[Anchovy fillets|anchovy fillets]], drained. Keep 3 back for the dressing as well as the reserved [[Oil|oil]]\n| 40 g (1.5 oz) [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly and finely [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n| 1 clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]] or [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[English mustard powder]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n| 150 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n| 2 slices of thick white [[Bread|bread]], crusts removed and cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 1 [[Clove garlic, crushed|clove garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[croutons]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], season with [[Black pepper|black pepper]], start the [[Garlic|garlic]] sizzling then add the cro\u00fbtons. Toss and [[Fry|fry]] until crispy and to taste\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Egg|egg]], [[Garlic|garlic]] clove, [[Lime juice|lime juice]], [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]], [[Worcestershire sauce]] and the 3 reserved [[Anchovies|anchovies]] and blend until smooth. Gradually drizzle the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] into the [[Blender|blender]] as though you were making mayonaise. As long as you don't rush adding the [[Oil|oil]], you should have a  [[Sauce|sauce]], the consistency of runny [[Salad|salad]]-[[Cream|cream]].\n}}\n'''Final assembly'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Finely chop the [[Anchovies|anchovies]]\n| Leaving the leaves whole, but ripping up very big leaves, layer the [[Salad|salad]] leaves and [[Anchovies|anchovies]]\n| Drizzle with the dressing and sprinkle with [[Parmesan]], finishing with the cro\u00fbtons.\n}}\n===Variations===\n*Add a handful of [[Wild rocket leaves|wild rocket leaves]] for a spicier [[Salad|salad]].\n*Add sliced cooked chicken or turkey for a more substantial meal.\n*Leave out the anchovies for a vegetarian version and use a vegetarian [[Worcestershire sauce]] - the original contains anchovies.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salad #oliveoil #worcestershiresauce #caesarsalad #anchovies #lettuce #egg #garlic #blackpepper #parmesancheese #croutons </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

Caesar Cardini (Italian-born [[Mexican]]) is credited with creating the salad.\n\nContrary to popular belief, the original Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] recipe did not contain pieces of [[Anchovy|anchovy]]; the slight anchovy flavour comes from the [[Worcestershire sauce]]. Cardini was opposed to using [[Anchovies|anchovies]] in his salad.\n\nIn the book From Julia Child's Kitchen, Julia Child describes how she ate a Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] at Cardini's restaurant when she was a child in 1920s, and some 50 years later she sought out and called Cardini's daughter, in order to discover the original recipe. In this recipe, [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves are served whole on the plate, because they are meant to be lifted by the stem and eaten with the fingers. It also calls for coddled [[Eggs|eggs]] and Italian [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nRather than re create the absolute original recipe, I have chosen to go for a composite of many current 'favourite' recipes.\n\n\n'''[[Salad]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 small cos [[Lettuce|lettuce]], washed and separated into leaves\n| 40 g (1.5 oz) [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly and finely [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n| 1 clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]] or [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[English mustard powder]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n| 150 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 slices of thick white [[Bread|bread]], crusts removed and cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 1 [[Clove garlic, crushed|clove garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[croutons]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], season with [[Black pepper|black pepper]], start the [[Garlic|garlic]] sizzling then add the cro\u00fbtons. Toss and [[Fry|fry]] until crispy and to taste\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Egg|egg]], [[Garlic|garlic]] clove, [[Lime juice|lime juice]], [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]], [[Worcestershire sauce]] and the 3 reserved [[Anchovies|anchovies]] and bland until smooth. Gradually drizzle the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] into the [[Blender|blender]] as though you were making [[mayonnaise]]. As long as you don't rush adding the [[Oil|oil]], you should have a  [[Sauce|sauce]], the consistency of runny [[Salad cream]].\n}}\n'''Final assembly'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Leaving the leaves whole, but ripping up very big leaves, layer the [[Salad|salad]] leaves and [[Anchovies|anchovies]]\n| Drizzle with the dressing and sprinkle with [[Parmesan]], finishing with the cro\u00fbtons.\n}}\n===Variations===\n*Add a handful of [[Wild rocket leaves|wild rocket leaves]] for a spicier [[Salad|salad]].\n*Add sliced cooked chicken or turkey for a more substantial meal.\n*For a vegetarian version use a vegetarian [[Worcestershire sauce]] - the original contains anchovies.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salad #oliveoil #worcestershiresauce #anchovies #lettuce #garlic #egg #croutons #parmesancheese #blackpepper #wildrocketleaves </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

Also, it is known to have been made without the [[Anchovies|anchovies]].  These were added much later to give the [[Sauce|sauce]] more body. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#thermomix #sauce #garlic #lemonjuice #mustard #mayonnaise #oliveoil #egg #parmesancheese #worcestershiresauce #grated </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Makes this recipe dead easy.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nI am experimenting with [[Spice|spice]] mixes from [[Taste Sensation Ltd]]; their Tex Mex marinade was wonderful so I arranged to get samples of their popular blends.\n\nAs this is an experiment I bought 1.4kg of [[pork shoulder]] and got the butcher to cut it into three slices.  This recipe uses one of those slices. I can use the other two to experiment with more of the [[Taste Sensation]] seasonings.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1400 g [[Pork shoulder|pork shoulder]]\n| 2 medium [[Red onions|red onions]], peeled and chopped\n| 1 [[Lemon|lemon]] cut into eight pieces\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning]]\n| 200 ml [[red wine]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[muscovado sugar]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Cajun Pulled Pork ready to cook.jpg|Ready to cook\nImage:Cajun Pulled Pork Ingredients.jpg|Minimal, but high quality ingredients\nImage:Taste Sensation spices with added cats.jpg|A sample of Taste Sensation spices, with added cats\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Squeeze the [[Lemon|lemon]] to collect the [[lemon juice]] while retaining the [[lemon]] pieces\n| Pour the red wine and lemon juice over the [[Pork|pork]]\n| Sprinkle the [[Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning]] over the pork\n| Line the [[Slow Cooker|slow cooker]] with the chopped [[Onions|onions]] and [[Lemon|lemon]] pieces\n| Lay the [[Pork shoulder|pork shoulder]] over the [[Lemon|lemon]] and [[Onions|onions]]\n| Sprinkle the [[muscovado sugar]] over everything\n| Slow cook on medium heat for 8 hours, turning now and then\n| If it looks to be drying out too much add a little extra liquid, water or beverage of your choice!\n| If you are able, about halfway through remove the rind and excess fat, together with the lemon pieces\n| After eight hours, shred the [[Pork|pork]] with two forks and mix into the gravy\n| Serve!\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThere are lots of great ways to serve [[Pulled pork|pulled pork]]:\n\n* In rolled up soft [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]] with crispy [[Lettuce|lettuce]] and [[Onions|onions]]\n\n* In [[Taco shells|taco shells]] with a [[Salad|salad]] mix and [[Sour cream|sour cream]]\n\n* As you would serve [[Roast pork|roast pork]]\n\n* As a [[Pizza topping|pizza topping]]\n\n* In a [[Burger|burger]] bun with a [[Salad|salad]]\n\n* As part of a [[Tapa|tapa]]\n===Chef's notes===\nThis was very, very good.  Impressed with the [[Cajun Seasoning]], not too hot but had tangy, herby notes. I needed to add a little extra liquid near the end, but only 50 ml or so. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lemon #cajunpulledpork #porkshoulder #onions #salad #pork #muscovadosugar #cajunseasoning #tapa #spice #redonions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Use it as a recipe template, almost any meat and certainly any favourite soup would work very well in this recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 5963\n|PortionCalories = 1490\n|DatePublished=1st March 2015\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Cheatin' pork enchiladas recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just, Wow!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is my [[Pork|pork]] version of [[Cheatin' chicken enchiladas]].  Use it as a recipe template, almost any [[Meat|meat]] and certainly any favourite [[Soup|soup]] would work very well in this recipe.\n\nIt requires pre cooked [[Pork|pork]], so I used [[Sous vide Tex-Mex pork tenderloin fillet]], however, you could easily slice a [[Pork tenderloin fillet|pork tenderloin fillet]] and pan [[Fry|fry]] it instead.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| About 700g of pre cooked [[Pork tenderloin fillet|pork tenderloin fillet]] - I used [[Sous vide Tex-Mex pork tenderloin fillet]]\n| 600g carton of Covent Garden Tennessee [[Pulled pork|pulled pork]] and [[Bean|bean]] [[Soup|soup]]\n| 50 g [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 8 [[Corn|corn]] or [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]]\n| 4 or 5 [[Spring onions, chopped|spring onions, chopped]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Old India Taco Seasoning]] or a similar [[Spice|spice]] [[Blend|blend]]\n| A splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] for the filling and a drizzle to [[Oil|oil]] the [[Baking|baking]] dish\n}}\n'''for the topping'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| A drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 50 g [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Pork fillet enchiladas baked.jpg|After 30 minutes at 180\u00b0 C \nImage:Pork fillet enchiladas soup added.jpg|Soup and cheese added\nImage:Pork fillet enchiladas rolled.jpg|8 pork Enchiladas, rolled\nImage:Pork fillet enchiladas ready to roll.jpg|Evenly filled and ready to roll\n</gallery>\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the filling ingredients to a bowl and mix really well.\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] the base of a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] with [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Distribute the filling amongst the 8 [[Tortillas|tortillas]], adding the filling to all of them before rolling up takes the guesswork out of the amount needed for each [[Tortilla|tortilla]].\n| Roll the [[Tortillas|tortillas]] up and starting at one end of the tray, lay them fold side down so they don't unroll.\n| Pour the [[Soup|soup]] over the [[Tortillas|tortillas]] and jiggle the pan to ensure it gets between the rolls.\n| Top with 50 g of [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]] a drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a grate of [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Salad|salad]] and a few sliced [[tomatoes]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#oliveoil #soup #cheddarcheese #tortillas #porktenderloinfillet #pork #grated #corn #pulledpork #miseenplace #tortilla </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

use other types of squash\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 25 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Squash type.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice dip</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great to use up your squash-glut.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] minutes until the [[Squash|squash]] starts to become soft..\n| Add the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] and [[Boil|boil]] for another 5 minutes\n| Drain well, return to the pan and mix in the [[Cream|cream]] [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Chillies|chillies]].\n| Blend to a paste with a hand liquidiser or [[Mash|mash]] really well.\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Sprinkle with fresh [[Parsley|parsley]] and serve.\n}}\n===Variations===\n\nWe make this with a variety of [[Squashes|squashes]], not just the [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]].\n\nUse [[Mascarpone|mascarpone]] [[Scoop]] out the flesh once soft.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#boil #cheese #cream #parsley #sweetcorn #squashes #squash #cheeseandchilisquashandsweetcorn #butternutsquash #mascarpone #boiledorsimmered </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Cheese and chilli cornbread a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheeseandchillicornbread #sweetcorn #onions #cheese #bakingpowder #bake #greaseproofpaper #eggs #cornbread #butter #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This savoury cornbread could be served as an accompaniment to a main course or barbecue, as a starter or just as a really nice savoury nibble\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3404\n|PortionCalories = 340\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 10\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Cheese and chilli cornbread recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasty, but heavy going</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.1</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice, but too much gives me indigestion - and I always eat too much!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis savoury [[Cornbread|cornbread]] could be served as an [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] to a [[Main course|main course]] or  [[Barbecue|barbecue]], as a [[Starter|starter]] or just as a really nice savoury nibble.  It is based on Jamie Oliver's recipe of the same name, though I recall having to adjust the quantities quite a bit from his original recipe.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 60 g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 2 large [[Onions|onions]], peeled and thinly sliced\n| 1 350g can of [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] kernels, drained\n| 4 large [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| 325 g coarse [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]]\n| 250 ml full [[Fat|fat]] [[Milk|milk]]\n| 1 heaped teaspoon [[Baking powder|baking powder]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| [[Sea Salt|Sea salt]] & [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 150 g strong [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 3 fresh [[Green chillies|green chillies]], 2 deseeded and chopped finely, the other cut into thin rings\n| [[Olive oil]] for greasing\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Butter|butter]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Wok|wok]], give it a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 15 minutes\n| Once the [[Onions|onions]] are golden, carefully add the drained [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]]\n| [[Stir-fry]] the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] for a few minutes then remove the pan from the heat and set to one side.\n| Add the [[Eggs|eggs]], [[milk]], [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]], [[Flour|flour]], [[Baking powder|baking powder]], a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and most of the [[Cheese|cheese]] (leaving a little to sprinkle on the top) and beat until really well mixed.\n| Stir in the onions and sweetcorn and mix again.  It helps to leave the mixure to rest for 10 minutes after the first mix to allow the cornmeal to soak up the milk.\n| Grease two 22cm round flan sandwich tins with a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]], line the base with [[Greaseproof paper|greaseproof paper]] and pour in the [[Cornbread|cornbread]] mixture.\n| [[Bake]] for 20 minutes then carefully remove from the oven and sprinkle the top with the remaining sliced [[Chilies|chilies]] and [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| [[Bake]] for a further 10 minutes.\n| Remove from the [[baking tray]] and allow to cool on a wire rack for 15 minutes before serving.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Cheese and chilli cornbread ready to bake.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Cheese and chilli cornbread, ready to bake\nImage:Cheese and chilli cornbread ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients for cheese and chilli cornbread\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot or cold\n===Chef's note===\nDon't forget the [[greaseproof paper]] or you will find it very hard to get the cornbread out of the tins. :-(\n==See also==\nThis recipe is based on a version of Jamie Olivers 'Chilli cheese cornbread' from ''Jamie's America'' ISBN 978-0718154769\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheeseandchillicornbread #sweetcorn #onions #cheese #bakingpowder #bake #greaseproofpaper #eggs #cornbread #butter #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Cheese pupusas (V)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Cheese pupusas a vegetarian cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#curtido #masaharina #cheddar #toasted #ricotta #tortilla #grated #cheeses #corntortillas #cheese #tortillas \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=These pupusas are stuffed corn-tortillas, usually served with a spicy coleslaw called curtido\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2232\n|PortionCalories = 279\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Cheese pupusa with curtido\n |Servings = Servings: 8 - Will fill about 8 pupusa\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Cheese pupusa recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Anything made with Masa Harina is good</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I love the flavour, it's so different.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA pupusa is a stuffed corn-tortilla, usually served with a spicy coleslaw called [[curtido]].\n\nPupusas are hand-made and thick. Like all [[corn tortillas]], they are made using [[masa harina]].  They originate from El Salvador.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 cups of [[grated]] [[cheese]] (use a mixture of [[cheeses]]; [[Cheddar]], [[Mozzarella]] and [[ricotta]])\n| 3 tablespoons of [[double cream]]\n| &#189; a cup of chopped [[spring onions]]\n| [[Sea salt]] to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Corn tortilla recipe|Make the tortillas as shown here]], but don't cook them yet\n| Mix all of the ingredients together to make a soft paste\n| Divide the mixture into balls, slightly larger than golf-balls and place each ball in the centre of the tortilla and press the mixture out, leaving a gap around the edge\n| Cover with another [[tortilla]] and press together to seal\n| Heat a griddle pan or heavy frying pan and wipe over with a lightly oiled kitchen towel\n| Cook each  pupusa until it is nicely [[toasted]].  This will take about 4 minutes a side\n| Keep warm while you cook the remaining pupusas\n}}\n===Chef's tip===\nServe with [[curtido]]\n===Serving suggestions===\nTo prevent the [[tortillas]] sticking to the press, place the 'golf-ball' inside a folded piece of [[Bake-O-Glide]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Starters|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Pupusa]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#curtido #masaharina #cheddar #toasted #ricotta #tortilla #grated #cheeses #corntortillas #cheese #tortillas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chicken jambalaya",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken jambalaya, | Cajun recipes from the cook's Wiki\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chickenjambalaya #chicken #stock #onion #bayleaf #celery #rice #worchestersauce #ham #butter #parsley \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Jambalaya always brings to mind the Carpenters song; Jambalaya (On the Bayou) - this is what they were singing about\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1847\n|PortionCalories = 307\n|DatePublished=2nd January 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Chicken jambalaya with chorizo\n|Servings = 6 people\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 2 hours 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes<br />(includes cooking a chicken)\n|CookTime = 1 hour\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken jambalaya recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">So this is what it is</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Until I first made this I had no idea what Jambalaya was.  It's nice - a one-pot rice dish.  Simples!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nJambalaya always brings to mind the Carpenters song; ''Jambalaya (On the Bayou)''  Not a Carpenters song but a dish traditionally made in one pot, with [[Meats|meats]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]]. It is completed by adding [[Stock|stock]] and [[Rice|rice]].  Looking at various recipes in more detail, this strikes me now as a typical leftover dish.  Cooking up what you have around at the time.\n===Making this your own recipe===\nWhen I made this for the first time, not having the slightest idea what jambalaya was, it looked quite complex, however, having made it many times now I now think it is probably one of the easiest recipes around. It is also a brilliant recipe to adapt to your own personal taste.  It is also an excellent recipe for using up leftovers.\n\nJust follow a few basic steps and you will be able to make you own version of this recipe.\n* Rinse the rice in cold running water first.\n* Fry the onions, garlic and vegetables first, plus any meat that might need more cooking than the rice does.\n* Ensure the rice is well coated in the oil before adding any stock.\n* Measure the stock by doubling the volume of the rice (4 cups of water to 2 cups of rice, etc.)\n* Don't add all of the stock at once, add more if it looks as though it will dry out before the rice is done.\n* If you have ingredients that don't need much cooking (prawns etc.) or vegetables that you want to serve with a bit of a crunch then add them during the last five minutes of cooking.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 x 2kg (4 lb) [[Chicken|chicken]], [[Parson's nose|parson's nose removed]]\n| A few [[Bay leaf|bay leaves]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], unpeeled, chopped into quarters\n| About 200 g from one or more of cooked meat\n| 40 g (1 &frac12; oz) [[Butter|butter]], [[ghee]] or [[olive oil]]\n| 4 to 7 [[Cloves garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 6 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Chopped on the diagonal|chopped on the diagonal]]\n| 2 sticks of [[Celery|celery]], 'strings' removed with a [[Mandoline|mandoline]] and chopped into moons\n| 3 or 4 sweet [[Bell peppers|bell peppers]], any colour, deseeded and chopped\n| 3 teaspoons [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]]\n| &#189; teaspoon of [[dried oregano]] or [[dried mixed herbs]]\n| 2 tablespoons fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], chopped, if available\n| 1 large can [[Plum|plum]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped\n| 500ml to 600 ml of the water the [[Chicken|chicken]] was [[Boiled|boiled]] in\n| 1 tablespoon [[Worcester sauce|Worcester sauce]]\n| [[Chillies]], [[chilli sauce]] or [[chilli powder]] to add warmth, not heat.\n|* I used: 1 teaspoon chili guajillo (powder), 2 teaspoons pasilla chili (diced), 1/2 a teaspoon of chipotle chillies (diced)\n|* Suggested alternative if using sauce: 1 to 2 tablespoons [[Louisiana hot pepper sauce]] (or to taste)\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 400 g (14 oz) [[Basmati rice|basmati rice]] ([[Long grain rice|long grain rice]])\n}}\n''' Garnish'''\n* Finely chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Remove any giblets, cut off and discard the [[Parson's nose]].\n| Wash the [[Chicken|chicken]] under cold running water, inside and out\n| Place the [[Chicken|chicken]] in a large pot and pour over just enough [[Boiling|boiling]] water to cover\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and the [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]] and [[Boil|boil]] for about 1 hour or until tender\n| Set the [[Chicken|chicken]] to one side, reserve the [[Stock|stock]] and discard the [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]] and [[Onion|onion]] quarters\n| Once chicken has cooled discard skin and bone\n| Heat the [[Butter|butter]] in a large pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] for a few minutes\n| Add the [[Ham|ham]], [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Celery|celery]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Saut\u00e9|saut\u00e9]] for 5 minutes\n| Rinse rice under cold running water for a few minutes until the water runs clear\n| Add the [[Rice|rice]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for a minute so the grains are coated by the oil\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]] (about 500 ml to start), [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Spices|spices]], [[Worcester sauce|Worcester sauce]], [[Hot pepper sauce|hot pepper sauce]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Chicken|chicken]]\n| Stir well, cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] on a very low hob until the liquid has gone and the [[Rice|rice]] is cooked.  Add a little more water if it dries out before the rice is done.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken jambalaya in pot.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Chicken jambalaya, ready to cook\nImage:Chicken jambalaya boil.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Chicken, ready to boil\n</gallery>\n===Variations===\nI raided the garden for anything to add to the chicken boil: a few [[carrots]], some [[leeks]] a few spare sticks of [[celery]] and bunches of [[parsley]].\n===Chef's notes===\nI have doubled the rice quantity from the original recipe as there was so little rice.  I have not quite doubled the stock quantity so keep an eye on the water level to ensure that it does not dry out.\n\nRather than using [[chili sauce]] for the heat I used a mixture of my [[Exotic chili powders]] to add more than just heat.  The quantities I used did not make this hot (like a chili), just a little warmth.\n\nThe [[stock]] left from cooking the chicken is really good quality so whatever you don't use, freeze in bags or cups far later use.\n\n==See also==\n* http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jambalaya\n* http://www.bbcgoodfood.com/recipes/1167651/chicken-and-chorizo-jambalaya\n* http://www.deliaonline.com/recipes/type-of-dish/one-pot-meals/chicken-jambalaya.html\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickenjambalaya #chicken #stock #onion #bayleaf #celery #rice #worchestersauce #ham #butter #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken jambalaya - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #sauce #bayleaf #rice #onion #thermomix #parsley #bacon #garlic #springonions #celery \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a chicken jamabalaya recipe for the Thermomix. The chicken is steamed in the Varoma basket, but can also be poached in the bowl at 90\u00b0\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1430\n|PortionCalories = 357\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 45 minutes \n|PrepTime = 25 minutes\n|CookTime = 1 hour 20 minutes \n|Image = [[Image:Chicken jambalaya (TM) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Just like the song</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..but Thermy-made!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a [[Chicken|chicken]] jamabalaya recipe for the [[Thermomix]].  The chicken is [[Steamed|steamed]] in the Varoma basket, but can also be [[Poached|poached]] in the bowl at 90\u00b0.\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 1 x 1.3kg [[Chicken|chicken]], [[parson's nose]] removed\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], cut into quarters\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, peeled\n| 30g [[Butter|butter]], [[Ghee|ghee]] or [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 100g cooked [[Bacon|bacon]]\n| 4 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Chopped on the diagonal|chopped on the diagonal]]\n| 2 sticks of [[Celery|celery]], chopped into half-moons\n| 2 [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], any colour, deseeded and chopped\n| 200g [[Basmati rice|basmati rice]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]] or [[Dried mixed herbs|dried mixed herbs]]\n| 2 tablespoons fresh [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]], chopped, if available\n| 1 400g tin [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]], chopped\n| 1 tablespoon Worcester [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| [[Chillies]], [[Chilli sauce|chilli sauce]] or [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] - I used 1 teaspoon extra [[Hot chilli powder|hot chilli powder]] and 1 tablespoon Nando's Piri-Piri [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| [[Parsley]], chopped (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Fill the TM bowl with 1.2kg water and add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]].\n| Place the [[Chicken|chicken]] in the Varoma basket '''30 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 2'''. \n| Turn [[Chicken|chicken]] over and continue cooking for another 30 minutes. \n| Check for done-ness and cook for longer if necessary. \n| Remove the basket and allow to cool, reserving the [[Steaming|steaming]] water and discarding the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]. \n| Remove the [[Meat|meat]] from the [[bones]]. \n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] to the bowl and chop '''5 seconds / Speed 5''' then scrape down the inside of the bowl. \n| Add the [[Butter|butter]] or [[Oil|oil]], [[Bacon|bacon]], [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Celery|celery]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and saut\u00e9e '''10 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1 / MC off'''. \n| Add the [[Rice|rice]] and cook for '''1 minute / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1 / MC off'''. \n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Spices|spices]], [[Herbs|herbs]], Worcester [[Sauce|sauce]], [[Hot pepper sauce|hot pepper sauce]] and [[Chicken|chicken]]. \n| Fill the bowl with the reserved [[Steaming|steaming]] water until you reach the 2 litre mark in the bowl.\n| Cook '''15 minutes  / 90\u00b0  / Speed Spoon / Reverse Blade''' or until the liquid has gone and the [[Rice|rice]] is cooked - it may help to remove the MC for part of the cooking time.\n| Add a little more water if it dries out before the [[Rice|rice]] is done. \n| Serve and garnish with the finely chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] if desired.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Adapted for [[Thermomix]] from [[User:Chef|Chef's]]'s recipe for [[Chicken jambalaya]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Jambalaya]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #sauce #bayleaf #rice #onion #thermomix #parsley #bacon #garlic #springonions #celery </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

seeds|pumpkin seeds]] until they start to pop, turn them often\n| Add them to a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade and grind them finely\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], quartered [[Onion|onion]], peeled [[garlic]], [[chillies]], [[cumin seeds]] and [[turmeric powder]] and blend to a paste\n| Finally add the [[peanut butter]] and the [[chicken stock]]\n| Meanwhile, heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a frying pan, add the [[lardons]] and the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] until the chicken is golden [[Brown|brown]]\n| Add the blended sauce to a large pan, title": "Chicken with pumpkins seeds and peanut butter (slow cooker recipe)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken with pumpkins seeds and peanut butter recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tomatoes #chicken #lardons #springonions #pumpkinseeds #garlic #parsley #onion #turmericpowder #peanutbutter #cuminseeds \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A nice Tex-Mex twist on a simple chicken stew. [[Onion|onion]], peeled [[garlic]], [[chillies]], [[cumin seeds]] and [[turmeric powder]] and blend to a paste\n| Finally add the [[peanut butter]] and the [[chicken stock]]\n| Meanwhile, heat the title": "Chilaquiles",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chilaquiles a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chilaquiles #chihuahuacheese #tortilla #chillipeppers #sourcream #sauce #onion #corntortillas #montereyjackcheese #tomatoes #garlic \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Chilaquiles are a traditional Mexican dish. Typically, corn tortillas cut in quarters and lightly fried are the base of the dish\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3897\n|PortionCalories = 974\n|DatePublished=8th August 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Chilaquiles - This looks weird, but it was really good! - My apologies to Catalina  and Ale!\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chilaquiles recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Better than it looks here</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Delicious and unusual.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]])</span></span>\n}}\n[[Chilaquiles]] are a traditional [[Mexican]] dish. Typically, [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] cut in quarters and lightly [[Fried|fried]] are the base of the dish. Green or red [[Salsa|salsa]] or [[Mole|mole]], is poured over the crisp [[Tortilla|tortilla]] triangles, called totopos. The mixture is [[Simmered|simmered]] until the tortilla starts softening. [[Eggs]] (scrambled or fried) and [[pulled chicken]] are sometimes added to the mix. The dish is topped with [[Cheese|cheese]] (typically grilled chihuahua  cheese ) and/or [[Sour cream|sour cream]] (crema), and it is served with [[Refried beans|refried beans]]. Like many dishes, regional and familiar variation are quite common.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 10 [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] cut up in triangles ([[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]])\n| &frac12; Cup of [[corn oil]]\n| 3 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| &frac12; [[Onion]]\n| 4 Medium Size [[Tomatoes]]\n| 3 [[Chilli peppers|chilli peppers]] (I suggest [[Serrano|Chile Serrano]])\n|* ''Serrano is classed as a hot chilli if you are looking for an equivalent''\n| 1 Cup of [[Sour cream|sour cream]] \n| 1 Cup of grated [[chihuahua cheese]] or [[Monterey Jack cheese]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of salt.\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| On a [[Deep frying|deep frying]] saucepan [[Fry|fry]] the [[Tortillas|tortillas]]\n| On a pot toast the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Chilli peppers|chilli peppers]],  [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]]. Liquidate the tomatoes, salt, [[Chilli peppers|chilli peppers]], onion and garlic.\n| As the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] is [[Frying|frying]] add the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| Let the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] dunk into the [[Sauce|sauce]] but make sure the [[Chips|chips]] don't get too soft.\n| Add the [[chihuahua  cheese]] and it will melt with the heat.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Sour cream|sour cream]] and grilled [[chihuahua cheese]] on top.\n===Chef's notes===\nYou may add [[Epazote leaves|epazote leaves]], to the [[Sauce|sauce]]!\n===recipe source===\n* ''By [[User:User:CatyGPadilla|Catalina Garcia]] and Ale Angeles from Mexico''\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you're making this in Europe, a mild [[white cheddar]] is a good substitute for [[chihuahua cheese]] or [[Monterey Jack cheese]].\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you want to do this en Ecuador, use ripe mozzarella cheese and you can use paico is the same that epazote (A.V)\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chilaquiles #chihuahuacheese #tortilla #chillipeppers #sourcream #sauce #onion #corntortillas #montereyjackcheese #tomatoes #garlic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| [[Vegetables]] as available ([[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Carrots|carrots]], [[Courgettes|courgettes]], for instance), chopped or sliced\n| 400g can chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 400g can [[Red kidney beans|red kidney beans]] in unsalted water, drained\n| 1 - 2 [[green chillies]], deseeded and chopped\n| 1 - 2 teaspoons [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]] (freshly ground is best)\n| 1 - 2 teaspoons [[Dried|dried]] [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| 1 square of Lindt 85% [[Chocolate|chocolate]], or equivalent dark chocolate: ([[Green & Blacks Organic Chocolate]])\n| 100ml [[Beef|beef]] [[Stock|stock]] (can be made from a cube if necessary)\n| [[Salt]] & [[Pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat a couple of tablespoons of [[Oil|oil]] in a saucepan.  [[Fry]] [[Onion|onion]].  After a few minutes add Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]].  Cover and continue [[Frying|frying]] until [[Onions|onions]] are translucent.\n| Add [[Meat|meat]] and [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add remaining ingredients and seasoning.\n| Bring to [[Boil|boil]].  Lower heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for  30mins to 1 hour, depending on how much you've made.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with [[Tortillas|tortillas]], [[Rice|rice]] or crusty [[Bread|bread]] and a side [[Salad|salad]].\n\n===Variations===\n\nBy increasing the proportion of [[Beans|beans]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]], one pack of [[Meat|meat]] can be stretched to ten or twelve servings.  If you do this, increase the proportion of [[Herbs|herbs]], [[Spices|spices]] and [[Chocolate|chocolate]] accordingly.  If you don't want to use chocolate (which really is the secret ingredient), you can substitute a little [[White sugar|white sugar]] to bring out the flavour of the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n\nIf you don't like food too spicy, cut down the green [[Chili|chili]] content.  I make it for my young son in this way and he loves it with [[Rice|rice]].\n\n===Chef's tip===\n\nI make a big pot a couple of times a year and each time freeze 15 - 18 double portions that can be microwaved quickly to give us a hot meal in about 15 mins at the end of the working day.  \n\nIf you use low-[[Fat|fat]] [[Beef|beef]], this meal is a healthy option, as it has no other source of [[saturated fat]] apart from the small amount of [[Chocolate|chocolate]].\n\n==See also==\n* {{ChiliConCarne}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beef #chocolate #onion #tomatoes #rice #vegetables #garlic #simmer #frying #tortillas #dried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Plain [[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]] or [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Pitta|pitta]] strips make a great dip for this dish.   Make your own [[tortilla chips]] if you have the time.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 fresh [[Green chillies|green chillies]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| &frac12; [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 2 fat cloves of [[Garlic]]\n| 250 g strong [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 250 g [[Jarlsberg cheese]] or [[Gruyere cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 50 ml [[Sour cream|sour cream]]\n| 150 ml [[Double cream|double cream]]\n| 2 large fresh [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 15 ml [[Tequila]]\n}}\n'''to serve '''\n* 200g Plain [[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]] or [[Pitta|pitta]] strips\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Scorch the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] and peel them using the technique shown here (for [[Red peppers|red peppers]])\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Rub the skins off the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] - use rubber gloves if your skin is sensitive and don't run your eyes!\n| Slice the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[chillies]] and scoop out and discard the [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| Cut the chillies and tomatoes into thin strips\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onions|onions]] for 5 minutes until soft\n| Turn down the heat and add the [[Cheese|cheese]], sour and [[Double cream|double cream]] and stir until the cheese has melted and combined.\n| Just before serving, mix in the [[Tequila|tequila]] and add the [[Tomato|tomato]] and [[Chilli|chilli]] strips.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe warm with [[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]].\n\nTry and use plain, unsalted [[tortilla chips]] as most commercial tortilla chips are coated with a disgusting powder that purports to be flavouring, which masks the delicious corn flavour. If you do,find them, let me know where you get them from!\n===Variations===\nPowder &frac14; teaspoon [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]] and &frac14; teaspoon [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]] in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]] and sprinkle onto the surface before serving.\n\nSprinkle a little homemade [[Tex-Mex seasoning]] on the surface.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortillachips #tomatoes #chilliesinagarlicandcheesesauce #chillies #garlic #tequila #doublecream #pitta #grated #jarlsbergcheese #cheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chilli beans",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chilli beans recipe Cooking with chillies\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chillibeans #beans #bread #chillipowder #redpepper #parsley #molasses #mustard #onion #maincourse #plumtomatoes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Another vegetarian chili offering for our Gent night\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1226\n|PortionCalories = 613\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Chilli beans & cold rice in moulds\n |Servings = Servings: 2 - Serve 2 as a [[Main course|main course]] with [[Bread|bread]] or [[Rice|rice]] or 4 as a side-dish\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chilli beans & cold rice moulds recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Pretty good, pretty food</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice idea for a veggy meal.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\nAnother vegetarian offering for our [http://www.guardian.co.uk/lifeandstyle/wordofmouth/2009/may/14/ghent-vegetarian-city-healthy-belgium Gent night].\n\nThis recipe is almost identical to '''The Fabulous Baker Brothers Beans recipe''' seen on Channel 4 recently.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 30 ml (2 tablespoons) [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]])\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 3 [[Cloves garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| &#189; to 1 teaspoon [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] or to taste\n| 1 x 400g (14 oz) can of [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]], chopped\n| 142 ml (&frac14; pint) [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 1 teaspoon whole [[Grain|grain]] [[Mustard|mustard]]\n| 15 ml (1 tablespoons) [[Black treacle|black treacle]] or dark [[Molasses|molasses]]\n| 1 x 425 g (15 oz) can [[Red kidney beans|red kidney beans]], rinsed and drained\n| 1 x 425 g (15 oz) can black eye [[Beans|beans]], rinsed and drained\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 tablespoon chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n'''to garnish'''\n* 1 small [[Red pepper|red pepper]] or a few spring onions, chopped (optional)\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan, give it a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and then saut\u00e9 the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] until it softens and starts to take some colour, about 5 minutes.\n| Sprinkle the [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] over the [[Onions|onions]] and mix well.\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Stock|stock]], [[Molasses|molasses]], [[mustard]] and the [[Beans|beans]].  Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] vigorously, uncovered for 15 minutes stirring now and then.  Simmer for longer if you want a thicker consistency.\n| Add the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] , taste and adjust the seasoning if necessary.  [[Simmer]] for a further 5 minutes.\n| [[Roasted red pepper|Roast the red pepper]], remove the seeds and pith and  chop into slices\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chilli beans reducing.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Chilli beans reducing\nImage:Chilli beans the ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Chilli beans, the ingredients\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nGarnish with chopped [[Red pepper|red pepper]], or [[Spring onions|spring onions]] and serve with [[Bread|bread]] or [[Boiled rice|boiled rice]].  The cold rice in moulds was an especially good contrast with this dish.\n===Variations===\nUse any variety of [[Beans|beans]] or [[Pulses|pulses]].  [[Chick peas]] are nice with this.\n==See also==\n* [[Boston baked beans]]\n* http://www.channel4.com/4food/recipes/tv-show-recipes/the-fabulous-baker-brothers-recipes/baker-brother-beans-recipe\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chillibeans #beans #bread #chillipowder #redpepper #parsley #molasses #mustard #onion #maincourse #plumtomatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chilli con carne (PC)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chilli con carne a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#diced #tomatoes #chilli #staranise #kidneybeans #beans #redwine #simmer #pressurecooker #butter #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe requires partial use of a pressure cooker\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2422\n|PortionCalories = 605\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime = 1 day, 4 hours, 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 day, 20 minutes\n|CookTime = 4 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Chilli con carne (PC) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Super tender</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The trick is using the pressure cooker</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n\n}}{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\nThis recipe requires partial use of a [[Pressure cooker|pressure cooker]].  Ideally, this should be made a day or two before you want to eat it, so that the flavours can develop more.\n\n'''For the [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 50g [[Salt|salt]] dissolved in 500ml tap water\n| 150g [[Dried|dried]] [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]]\n| 500g [[Cherry tomatoes|cherry tomatoes]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Chilli|chilli]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 450g [[Minced beef|minced beef]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and [[diced]]\n| 2 [[Star anise|star anise]]\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]], peeled and [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely chopped\n| [[Green chillies]] to taste, chopped (remove [[Seeds|seeds]] if desired, but personally I don't bother)\n| 30g [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e\n| 375ml [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| 50g [[Heston's spiced butter]]\n| 3 medium [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 500ml [[Beef Stock|beef stock]]\n}}\n'''To finish and serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 [[Red peppers|red peppers]], de-seeded, [[Roasted|roasted]] and peeled\n| Seasoning\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Put the [[Brine|brine]] ([[Salt|salt]] and water mixture) in the bowl with the [[Beans|beans]]. \n* Cover and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for 12 hours\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and 50g water into a [[Pressure cooker|pressure cooker]]\n| Put on the lid, bring to pressure over a high heat, reduce heat and cook for 20minutes\n| Remove from the heat and allow to cool before opening the lid\n| Put the pan on a high heat, stirring frequently until the liquid is reduced by half - about 10 minutes\n| Drain the [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]] and add to the pan.\n| Add enough water to cover the [[Beans|beans]] if necessary.\n| Replace the lid and bring up to pressure over a high heat.\n| Reduce and heat and cook for 20 minutes.\n| Leave the mixture until completely before opening.\n| Meanwhile, to start the [[Chilli|chilli]], coat the bottom of a large pan with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and place over a high heat until [[Smoking|smoking]].\n| Add the [[Mince|mince]], in batches if necessary, so that it browns rather than [[Stews|stews]].\n| Remove and drain the [[Meat|meat]].\n| Add a little water to the pan to [[Deglaze|deglaze]] it, and tip the water and bits in with the drained [[Meat|meat]].\n| Reduce the heat to medium-high and thinly coat with another layer of [[Oil|oil]].\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and the [[Star anise|star anise]] and cook for 7-10 minutes until the onion begins to colour.\n| Add the [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Green chillies|green chillies]] and cook for another 10 minutes or until the carrot is soft.\n| Add the [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e, stir and cook for another 5 minutes until everything turns a brick-red colour.\n| Pour in the [[Red wine|red wine]] and allow to reduce by two thirds.\n| Remove the [[Star anise|star anise]] and discard.\n| Stir in the spiced [[Butter|butter]], the [[Mince|mince]], [[Diced|diced]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Stock|stock]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] over a low heat for 2-3 hours, stirring occasionally.\n| To finish, fold the [[Beans|beans]] and chopped [[Peppers|peppers]] into the [[Chilli|chilli]] and bring to a [[Simmer|simmer]].\n| Season and stir in more spiced [[Butter|butter]] to increase the heat.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Rice|rice]], or [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Sour cream|sour cream]] \n===Recipe source===\n* Lightly adapted from a recipe in Heston Blumenthal at Home ISBN 1408804409\n===Chef's notes===\nMy husband felt that it needed 5 chillies, rather than 2.  Also there was too much liquid, possibly caused by the fact that during simmering, it was covered for most of the time.\n===See also===\n* {{ChiliConCarne}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Pressure cooker recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#diced #tomatoes #chilli #staranise #kidneybeans #beans #redwine #simmer #pressurecooker #butter #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
