                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chilli gravy, Barbecue recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chilligravy #onion #oliveoil #gravy #lardons #onions #stock #simmer #ground #masaharina #chillies \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=OK chilli freaks, here's a chance to excel!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 865\n|PortionCalories = 216\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 4 - Makes 4 cups of [[Chilli|chilli]] [[Gravy|gravy]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 55 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 50 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chilli gravy recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Mmmm; chillies</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Saves me having to add chilli to normal gravy.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\nOK [[Chilli|chilli]] freaks, here's a chance to excel!  In common with [[Chillies|chillies]], chilli gravy goes with just about anything.\n\nIt is great over any [[Barbecued|barbecued]] [[Meats|meats]] and [[Sausages|sausages]] and mandatory for [[Tex-Mex]] meals.\n\nThe beauty is that you can tailor the flavours to suit your tastes.  It also freezes well in 'meal-sized' portions.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]] (or the less healthy [[Lard|lard]] option!)\n| 2 big [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]].\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced.\n| 2 tablespoons [[Lardons|lardons]] (or [[Home smoked bacon|home smoked bacon]], chopped).\n| Your own variety of [[Dried|dried]] [[Chillies|chillies]], powdered in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]]\n| &frac14; teaspoon [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]]\n| &frac14; teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| 2 cups water\n| 2 cups [[Beef stock|beef stock]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Masa harina|masa harina]]\n| [[Sea salt]] to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Lardons|lardons]] on a medium heat in the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until soft, about 7 minutes.\n| Add the [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spice|spice]] and mix well.\n| Add the liquids, just bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and immediately reduce to a [[Simmer|simmer]] and cook, uncovered for 30 minutes.\n| Use a little of the [[Stock|stock]] to mix the [[Masa harina|masa harina]] to a paste and then add back into the stock, whisk well and [[Simmer|simmer]] for another 10 minutes.\n| Taste and season with [[Salt|salt]] if required.\n}}\n===Variations===\nCheat, cheat, cheat!\n\nI found half a pot of commercial [[Onion|onion]] [[Gravy|gravy]] in the [[Freezer|freezer]] which prompted this recipe. (I wanted something to liven up some [[Meatballs|meatballs]]).\n\nIf you are starting with a ready-made ([[Onion|onion]]) [[Gravy|gravy]], just omit the [[olive oil]], [[lardons]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Stock|stock]] and water.\n===Chef's note===\nProbably not at all authentic, but the juice of 1 [[lime]], 2 teaspoons of [[brown sugar]] and a tablespoon of [[tomato puree]] rounds this off nicely.\n==See also==\n* Many other [[gravy recipes]]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chilligravy #onion #oliveoil #gravy #lardons #onions #stock #simmer #ground #masaharina #chillies </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chorizo sausage, a Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pork #chili #chillies #poblano #porkfillet #groundcinnamon #smokedpaprikapowder #chorizosausages #vinegar #chilipowder #blender \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=When making this recipe I use the chorizo sausages immediately (as they are so good)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1081\n|PortionCalories = 180\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6 - Makes 4 large sausages \n |Difficulty = 3\n |ImageComment = Chorizo sausages, the real McCoy\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chorizo.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">What a fiddle</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">They were tasty though, and I like the idea of chorizo 'hamburgers'</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nWhen making this recipe I use the [[Chorizo sausages|chorizo sausages]] immediately (as they are so good).  I have not tried drying or [[Preserving|preserving]] them in any way, though I guess it would be possible with this recipe. For this reason, I don't bother to get the casings, I just make the [[sausages]] like patties or burgers.\n\nUse these in [[:Special:Whatlinkshere/Chorizo_sausage|any recipe that calls for chorizo sausages]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.5 tablespoons [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n| 1 large [[Dried|dried]] [[Poblano|poblano]] [[Chili|chili]], stalk removed\n| 4 fresh [[Habanero|habanero]] [[Chillies|chillies]], stlaks removed or 3 teaspoons hot [[Chili powder|chili powder]]\n| 675 g (1.5 lb) lean [[Pork|pork]] ([[Pork fillet|pork fillet]] is good here) , chopped coarsely\n| 1 tablespoon fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], chopped\n| 6 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]] or [[Smoked paprika powder|smoked paprika powder]] if you can find it\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Ground cloves|ground cloves]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Spices|spices]], [[Chillies|chillies]] and the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] to a small [[Blender|blender]] attachment and grind to a paste.  A [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]] will do the job, just takes a bit more work!\n| Add the [[Pork|pork]] and the [[Spice|spice]] paste to a [[Food processor|food processor]] and pulse blend until you have a coarse mix.  Don't overdo this or you will end up with [[Pate|pate]] which is not what you need\n| Roll into [[Sausage|sausage]] shapes or flat patties\n| Preheat the oven to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5)\n| Cook for 20 minutes on a lightly oiled oven tray\n| Verify the [[Meat|meat]] is cooked properly as it is [[Pork|pork]] remember\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot or cold\n\n===Variations===\nAdjust the amount of [[Chili|chili]] to your personal taste.  I like mine quite hot.\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pork #chili #chillies #poblano #porkfillet #groundcinnamon #smokedpaprikapowder #chorizosausages #vinegar #chilipowder #blender </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

gas 6) Grease a 23 cm (9 \") [[baking tray]] with melted [[Butter|butter]] or [[Ghee|ghee]]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large bowl, mix all the ingredients together except for the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] kernels.  Continue mixing until you have a smooth, even [[batter]]\n| Drain the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]], add to the mixture and mix well to combine the kernels\n| Pour into the greased pan and [[Bake|bake]] for about 20 minutes at the top of the oven\n| It should be golden [[Brown|brown]] and springy to the touch\n| Allow to cool for 15 minutes before attempting to cut\n}}\n===Variations===\nFor a hot cheesy [[Cornbread|cornbread]], add 110 g (4 oz) of [[Shredded|shredded]] [[Cheddar]] or [[Monterey Jack|Monterey Jack cheese]] and a big handful of drained, [[pickled jalape\u00f1o chillies]] - yum!\n==See also==\n*[[Quick cornbread]] - 25 minutes from larder to table - from Nik and Edwina's Cookbook\n*[[Cheese and chilli cornbread]] - The perfect combination\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sweetcorn #ghee #cornbread #butter #batter #bakingpowder #miseenplace #montereyjack #masaharina #quickcornbread #gumbo </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Cover and simmer until the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] are cooked\n| Remove from the heat and leave to stand for 1 hour\n| Blend about a quarter of the chowder until smooth and mix back into the pan\n| Reheat and serve, garnished with the [[Fried|fried]] [[Bacon|bacon]]\n}}\n===Variations===\nStir in a little [[Double cream|double cream]] for a really luxurious chowder\nAdd [[Smoked fish|smoked fish]], [[Crab|crab]], [[Crayfish|crayfish]], or [[Clams|clams]] for a nice fishy chowder\n[[Chilli flakes]] and chopped [[Pickled|pickled]] jalape\u00f1os as a garnish make a nice spicy chowder \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bacon #cornchowder #potatoes #fry #fat #doublecream #boil #clams #crayfish #crab #rosemary </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Makes about 10 [[tortillas]]\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 35 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Tortilla press2.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Delicious</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I love the special aroma of anything made with masa</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThese delicious [[corn tortillas]] are easy to make, though best made with a [[tortilla press]] if you can get hold of one.\n\nYou '''must''' use [[masa harina]] as [[cornmeal]] will not work.\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 250g [[masa harina]]\n| 330 ml hot water\n| 1/2 a teaspoon table [[salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place all of the ingredients into the bowl '''10 seconds / Speed 7''', then '''1 minute / Knead'''.\n| Rest for at least 1 hour then shape into 10 equal sized balls.\n| Using a [[tortilla press]] or [[rolling pin]], place a ball of dough between two non-stick sheets ([[Bake-O-Glide]] or similar) and press into shape\n| Heat a frying pan to a medium high temperature (but with no oil).\n| Cook each tortilla on one side for 15 seconds.\n| Turn and cook for 45 seconds.\n| Turn again and cook for a further 15 seconds.\n| They should have brown speckles.\n}}\n===Serving suggestion===\n\nCan be eaten as they are, fried, wrapped around [[beans]], [[salad]], [[chicken]], [[cheese]] etc.\n\nUse as suggested in your recipe\n*Make [[Cheese pupusas]] or [[Dobladas]] with your homemade [[maize tortillas]]\n===Variations===\n\nAdd 1-2 teaspoons [[chilli powder]] and/or 2-3 teaspoons [[garlic powder]] to the mixture.\n\n===Chef's note===\n\nIf you don't have a [[tortilla press]], use 2 chopping boards or just two sheets of wood as a substitute.  Place each ball of [[dough]] between two non-stick surfaces such as small squares of [[Bake-O-Glide]] and stand on them!\n\n===Suppliers===\n\nSee the [[Tortilla Press]] page for UK suppliers.\n\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Starters|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortillapress #masaharina #dobladas #chillipowder #salad #tortillas #garlicpowder #maizetortillas #dough #cheesepupusas #thermomixrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Place ball of [[dough]] between two non-stick surfaces such as small squares of [[Bake-O-Glide]] and stand on them!\n\n===Suppliers===\n\nSee the [[Tortilla Press]] page for UK suppliers.\n\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Starters|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Tortilla]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortillapress #masaharina #dough #corntortillarecipe #dobladas #salad #rollingpin #tortillas #garlicpowder #chicken #beans </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

each cob, thick end down on a cutting board and with a sharp knife, cutting close to the cob, strip the kernels off.\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] in a saucepan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[onion]] for 5 to 6 minutes on a low heat until translucent.\n| Add the kernels and cook for 4 to 5 minutes, no more or they will harden.\n| Chop the [[Chilies|chilies]] and add to the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] mix.\n| Add the soft [[Cheese|cheese]] and the [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan]] and cook, stirring, until the cheese has melted.\n| Season to taste and serve with shavings or [[Parmesan cheese]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and teaspoon ground [[Ginger|ginger]]\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Grated|grated]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| Sea [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 160 g (5 oz) [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 100 ml (4 fl oz) strong [[Beef|beef]] [[Stock|stock]]\n| 3 [[Cloves|cloves]] of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed.\n| 360 g (12 oz) wild [[Crayfish|crayfish]] tails, chopped finely\n| 3 hard [[Boiled|boiled]] [[Eggs|eggs]], chilled and chopped\n| 1 tablespoon [[Cornflour|cornflour]], dissolved in 1 tablespoon water\n| 4 tablespoons plain [[Flour|flour]], seasoned with [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Crispy crayfish patties fridge ready.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready for the fridge (half quantity)\nImage:Crispy crayfish patties mixture.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Cooking the mixture (half quantity)\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Olive|olive]] [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Wok|wok]] and [[Fry|fry]] the spring [[Onions|onions]], [[Celery|celery]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes.\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]], [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]], [[Ginger|ginger]] and the Louisiana hot [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| Add the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]], [[Stock|stock]], chopped [[Crawfish|crawfish]] tails, chopped [[Eggs|eggs]] and the [[Cornflour|cornflour]] paste.\n| Mix well then remove from the heat.\n| Pat into small cakes, allow to cool then refrigerate for at least 1 hour.\n| [[Dip]] into the seasoned [[Flour|flour]] and [[Fry|fry]] in [[Butter|butter]] until crispy.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe hot with a [[Green salad|green salad]], [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] and [[Wedges|wedges]] of [[Lime|lime]].\n\n===Chef's note===\n\nBecause of the egg whites, these cracked and popped a bit whilst being fried.  I think the next time, I will roll save a little of the breading, dip them in egg and coat with a final layer of breading so the did not explode whilst cooking!\n\n===Alternatives===\n\nI bulked out the breadcrumbs with 50 % cornflakes, oats would be good too.\n==See also==\n{{Template:Crayfish recipes}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#crispycrayfishpatties #crayfish #garlic #flour #sauce #breadcrumbs #mayonnaise #eggs #olive #blackpepper #cornflour </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Hot and spicy.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Duck fajitas recipe.jpg|thumb|300px|right|A splash of sherry]]\nAn unusual slant on the [[Mexican]] favourite.  Serve this with '''[[cherry salsa]]''', chopped [[avocados]], [[spring onions]] and [[cucumbers]] and you will have an exceptional evening meal.  As it's a Mexican variation of [[crispy duck pancakes]] there is nothing to stop you using [[Chinese pancakes]] for this dish (except you can get more in a [[tortilla]]!)\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 [[duck]] breasts with skin\n| 150 g (5 oz)  [[Monterey Jack cheese]], [[grated]]\n| 1 [[red onion]], sliced\n| 2 [[sweet peppers]] of any colour, de-seeded and sliced\n| 2 small hot [[red chillies]], deseeded and sliced into rings\n| Pinch of [[cayenne pepper]]\n| &#188; teaspoon of [[dried]] [[oregano]]\n| &#189; teaspoon ground [[white cumin]] seeds\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Garlic|garlic]] powder or [[dried minced garlic]] (ground)\n| Splash of [[dry sherry]]\n| 1 Packet of [[corn tortillas]]\n| 2 large [[spring onions]], [[sliced on the diagonal]]\n}}\n\n1/2 [[cucumber]], peeled and [[julienned]] or quartered lengthwise and sliced in a [[food processor]]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| With a very sharp knife, cut a few slashes in the skin of the [[duck]]\n| Place the [[duck]], skin-side down in a cold [[frying]] pan and cook for 10 minutes on a medium heat, regularly draining any excess [[fat]].\n| Flip the breasts over and cook for another 10 minutes or so, until nicely [[seared]]. Duck is ok to eat rare.\n| Remove and rest for 5 minutes\n| Cut the [[duck]] width-wise into slices\n| Heat the pan, with a little [[oil]] until, add the [[peppers]] and [[onions]] and and [[fry]] on a high heat for about 4 minutes. Add all but the [[sherry]] and spring onions and [[stir-fry]] for a few minutes\n| Add a good splash of [[sherry]] and stir to de-glaze the pan.\n| Place the duck mixture in a serving bowl\n| Assemble the pancakes [[How to make crispy aromatic duck at home|like this]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nBring the [[tortillas]], duck mixture, [[lime wedges]], grated cheese, chopped [[avocados]], [[spring onions]] and [[cucumber]] slices to the table and let everyone make their own tortillas.\n\n===Chef's tip===\n\nIf using legs (I could not get breasts on the day I made this) you will probably be better cooking in an oven - they take so much longer because you don't get good contact with the pan as you do with breasts. 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4) for 45 minutes.\n\nDuck is OK to eat rare.  I remember being muttered at by the ''charming'' waiter at in a French restaurant when asking for duck (breasts) ''bien cuit''!\n\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Duck]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#duckfajitas #duck #springonions #sherry #avocados #cucumber #onions #montereyjackcheese #whitecumin #grated #limewedges </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Enfrijoladas recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Enfrijoladas recipe Cheese, from Cookipedia.Co.Uk\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#enfrijoladasrecipe #chorizo #garlicoliveoil #tortilla #grapefruitsalsa #corntortillas #tortillas #refriedbeans #sourcream #montereyjack #cheddarcheese \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Enfrijoladas is a Tex-Mex dish that is similar to enchiladas\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3828\n|PortionCalories = 957\n|DatePublished=2nd April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|ImageComment = Covered with melted [[Emmental]]\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 5 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 50 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Enfrijoladas recipe 2.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tex Max at home</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This was easy to make and tasted fabulous - thank you!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nEnfrijoladas is a [[Tex-Mex]] dish that is similar to [[enchiladas]].  The [[tortillas]] are slightly [[fried]] and filled with [[frijoles refritos]] ([[refried beans]]) and [[pork]], or in this recipe spicy [[chorizo]].  I cheated with the refried beans as I didn't have time to soak them so I used canned, which are ok if but a little too salty.  I used [[Emmental cheese]], which is not authentic but I though it would work well. It did. This dish was a huge success.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 8 [[corn tortillas]]\n| 2 cans refried beans (or [[Refried beans recipe|homemade refried beans]])\n| 110 g (4 oz) [[grated]] [[Emmenthal cheese]], [[Monterey Jack]] or [[Cheddar cheese]]\n| 1/2 a small jar of [[Jalape\u00f1os|pickled jalape\u00f1os chillies]] or to taste\n| 150 ml to 200 ml (1/4 pint +) of [[beef stock|beef]] or [[vegetable stock]] \n| 120 g (4 oz) or a packet of spicy [[chorizo]], sliced\n| A handful of fresh [[coriander]], chopped\n| 8 tablespoons [[sour cream]]\n| [[Garlic olive oil]] for frying the [[corn tortillas]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4)\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a frying pan heat a few drops of [[garlic olive oil]] and fry each [[tortilla]] for a minute or so a side.\n| So you don't use too much oil, turn the first one over after a minute, put the next uncooked one on top of this to soak a little of the oil, flip them both. Remove the cooked one and repeat until they are all done. Add a few more drops of olive oil if the pan is too dry.\n| Divide the [[chorizo]] the cold contents of one cans of [[refried beans]] and layer each [[tortilla]] with an equal share as in the photo.\n| Lay them in an ovenproof dish\n| Heat the remaining tin of beans and add enough [[stock]] to make them ''pourable''. This way the bean ''sauce'' can get between the tortillas. Stir in the [[pickled jalape\u00f1os]]\n| Pour the bean mixture between the [[tortillas]], add a drizzle of [[garlic olive oil]] over the top and cover with the grated cheese\n| Bake in the over for 30 minutes and finish under the grill if you like your cheese toasty\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Enfrijoladas recipe 1.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Fill each tortilla with chorizo and refried beans\nImage:Grapefruit salsa.jpg|thumb|300px|right|[[Grapefruit salsa]]\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nGarnish with a dollop of [[sour cream]] on top and a sprinkle of coriander.\n\nDon your big hat and serve with a [[grapefruit salsa]] or [[curtido]] and a glass of ice-cold San Miguel!\n\n''The Mexican way: A tip from one of our Mexican visitors'' - You can also fill your enfrijoladas with shredded chicken and sprinkle some chopped or thinly sliced onion on top.  \n\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#enfrijoladasrecipe #chorizo #garlicoliveoil #tortilla #grapefruitsalsa #corntortillas #tortillas #refriedbeans #sourcream #montereyjack #cheddarcheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Frito pie a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fritopie #cheese #onion #beef #sourcream #chili #tacoseasoning #tomatoes #grated #orange #cheesenachos \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A Frito pie typically consists of a small single-serving bag of Fritos (plain corn chips / tortilla chips), with a cup of chili poured over the top\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4148\n|PortionCalories = 1037\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 30 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Frito pie recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Sometimes, the simple things are the best.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This is one of those times!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA Frito pie typically consists of a small single-serving bag of Fritos (plain [[corn]] [[chips]] / [[tortilla chips]]), with a cup of [[chili]] poured over the top, usually finished up with [[grated]] [[cheese]] or [[onions]] and jalape\u00f1os and [[sour cream]]. Frito pies are popular in the Southwestern United States. \n\nThis dish is similar to [[Cheese nachos]] and the original [[Easy frito pie]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 150 g Fritos or other [[Tortilla chips|corn (maize) chips]]\n| &frac34; cup (175 ml) chopped [[onion]]\n| 2 [[tomatoes]], chopped\n| 1 cup (240 ml) [[grated]] [[cheddar cheese]]\n| 1 pound of ground [[beef]]\n| [[taco seasoning]]\n| 2&frac12; cups (590 ml) chili (homemade or canned)\n| 125 ml carton of [[sour cream]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Brown]] the ground [[beef]] and season according to [[taco seasoning]] mix.\n| Preheat oven to 350\u00b0 F (175\u00b0 C).\n| Spread 2 cups of Fritos in a [[baking]] dish.\n| Sprinkle half the [[onion]] , half the [[cheese]] and the chopped [[tomatoes]] over the Fritos.\n| Combine ground [[beef]] with the [[chili]] and pour over the [[onion]] and [[cheese]].\n| Sprinkle the remaining Fritos, [[onion]] and [[cheese]] over the [[chili]].\n| [[Bake]] for 15 or 20 minutes and [[cheese]] is bubbly.\n| Serve hot, garnish with [[sour cream]].\n}}\n===Variations===\n\nSee [[Easy frito pie|Quick and easy frito pie]]\n\n===Serving suggestion===\nScatter a handful of [[Jalape\u00f1os|pickled jalape\u00f1os]] over the top of the [[tortillas|tortilla chips]] before baking.\n\nAn [[orange]] cut into thin segments (skin on) and baked separately makes an nice refreshing accompaniment to this dish.\n\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Pies tarts and flans]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fritopie #cheese #onion #beef #sourcream #chili #tacoseasoning #tomatoes #grated #orange #cheesenachos </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Gambas al ajillo",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Gambas al ajillo, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#gambasalajillo #prawns #chickpeas #parsley #groundblackpepper #chiliflakes #garlic #lime #paprikapowder #prawn #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Gambas al ajillo or Garlic prawns. This could be a tapas dish, a starter, or if you doubled the amount, a main course\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 654\n|PortionCalories = 163\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = thumb|right|Gambas al ajillo, these beauties with garlic shoots\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Gambas al ajillo.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">More garlic please</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Food for the garlic fiend!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nGambas al ajillo or Garlic prawns.  This could be a [[tapas]] dish, a [[starter]], or if you doubled the amount, a [[main course]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450g (1 lb) fresh peeled [[prawns]]\n| 4 cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], crushed\n| 1 teaspoon hot [[chili flakes]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[smoked paprika]] powder (normal [[paprika powder]] will do)\n| 4 tablespoons [[dry sherry]]\n| 3 tablespoons freshly chopped [[parsley]]\n| Juice of 1 [[lemon]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 [[lime]], quartered\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly [[ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut each slice down the centre of the back of each [[prawn]].  This will enable you to remove the bitter black 'backbone' and will allow the [[prawn]] to  curl open when cooked.\n| Add 2 or 3 good glugs of [[olive oil]] to a large frying pan over a medium heat\n| When the oil is hot, but not smoking, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[chili flakes]] and saut\u00e9 for a few minutes so the oil is nicely flavoured. Don't burn the garlic or you will need to start again!\n| Turn up the heat and add the [[sherry]], [[lemon juice]], [[paprika powder]] and the [[prawns]], stirring until the [[prawns]] change colour and curl. This should take about 3 minutes\n| Arrange in a bowl and garnish with the chopped [[parsley]]\n| Season with [[sea salt]] and freshly [[ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with freshly baked [[bread]] and [[lime]] quarters\n[[Image:Boiled chickpeas.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Plain boiled [[chickpeas]] are a great way of adding healthy fibre to this dish]]\nIn a nod towards the recent report that [https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/health-46827426 we are not eating enough lifesaving fibre], we have started to add plain boiled [[chickpeas]] to lots of our meals.\nThis recipe is ideally suited to such an addition.  Just drop a fistfull of cooked chickpeas into the bowl as you serve the garlic prawns.  The bland-nuttiness works extremely well with the garlic oil.\nIt's worth trying, drained, canned [[chickpeas]] would be just as good as freshly cooked chickpeas. \n\n===Variations===\n\nThis can be made will unpeeled [[prawns]] or even [[defrosted]] frozen [[king prawns]].\n==See also==\n* [[Menorcan garlic prawns]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Starters|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Tapas,_mezze_and_antipasti|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#gambasalajillo #prawns #chickpeas #parsley #groundblackpepper #chiliflakes #garlic #lime #paprikapowder #prawn #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Garlic fried chicken with a masa harina crust",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Garlic fried chicken with a masa harina crust recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #garlicfriedchickenwithamasaharinacrust #eggwhites #blackpepper #marinade #cornflour #refrigerate #cup #lemonjuice #masaharina #accompaniment \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=It is years since I deep-fried anything so this is almost new territory for me. Reading one of Ken Homs early cookbooks gave me the impetus to try\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1765\n|PortionCalories = 882\n|DatePublished=8th March 2015\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = An unusual accompaniment of garlic mushrooms and grilled tomatoes\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  3 hours, 18 minutes\n|PrepTime =  3 hours, 10 minutes\n|CookTime =  8 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Garlic fried chicken with a masa harina crust.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Air frying is nicer</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A few years ago this would have been great, but now I can get the same results using an air-fryer and a spray of olive oil.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\n\nIt is years since I [[deep-fried]] anything so this is almost new territory for me.  Reading one of Ken Hom's early cookbooks gave me the impetus to try it again.  I'm glad I did, it was really good and not at all greasy.\n\nThis is really an aide-memoir for me; next time I would add a tablespoon of [[Old India Taco Seasoning]] for a bit more [[Spice|spice]], and I would also hammer the [[Chicken|chicken]] flat before slicing up.  This would enable less [[Oil|oil]] to be used (not so wasteful), and it would also give a shorter, more uniform cooking time. As it was, we had to cook all of the chicken pieces a little longer to be sure the largest pieces were properly cooked.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 400g small [[Chicken|chicken]] fillets\n| 1 tablespoon [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Shaoxing rice wine|shaoxing rice wine]] [[Vinegar|vinegar]] - [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]] will be fine \n| 3 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| A pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 2 [[Egg whites|egg whites]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n| 1 [[Cup|cup]] [[Masa Harina|masa harina]]\n| 1 to 2 cups [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Cut the [[Chicken|chicken]] fillets into bite-sized pieces\n* Add to a [[Lock & Lock box]] together with the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]], [[Rice|rice]] [[Wine vinegar|wine vinegar]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n* Shake well to mix and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for an hour or more to allow the [[Marinade|marinade]] to penetrate the [[Meat|meat]].\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Garlic fried chicken with a masa harina crust frying.jpg|Frying in a wok\nImage:Chicken coated with masa.jpg|Coated with masa harina after the egg-white and cornflour stage\nImage:Garlic fried chicken marinading.jpg|Marinade for an hour or more\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Drain the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces in a [[Colander|colander]] and discard the [[Marinade|marinade]] juices.\n| Whisk the [[Egg whites|egg whites]] and [[Cornflour|cornflour]] in a bowl.\n| Add the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces to the bowl and mix well. [[Refrigerate]] for 30 minutes.\n| Add the [[Cup|cup]] of [[Masa Harina|masa harina]] to a dry [[Lock and Lock box]], close the lid and shake hard to coat the [[Chicken|chicken]].\n| Heat a [[Wok|wok]] or [[Frying pan|frying pan]] with enough [[Oil|oil]] to just cover the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces.\n| Heat to 176\u00b0 C [350\u00b0 F] (a 2.5cm [1\"] cube of [[Bread|bread]] should [[Brown|brown]] in 60 seconds.\n| [[Fry]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces in 2 batches for about 4 minutes each batch.  Cut one of the largest pieces open to check that it is properly cooked.\n| Serve immediately.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n[[Chips]] and [[Salad|salad]] is probably the most usual [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] for this.  We had this with an unusual, but fantastic combination; [[Stuffed mushrooms with garlic and Parmesan|garlic mushrooms]] and [[Grilled|grilled]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #garlicfriedchickenwithamasaharinacrust #eggwhites #blackpepper #marinade #cornflour #refrigerate #cup #lemonjuice #masaharina #accompaniment </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Gas Mk 4 - Moderate/Medium)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large bowl, with a wooden spoon or a [[Hand mixer|hand mixer]] combine the melted [[Butter|butter]], 1 teaspoon [[Vanilla extract|vanilla extract]] and 2 of the [[Eggs|eggs]] into an even mixture\n| Lightly grease or spray a 23 cm x 33 cm (9\" x 13\") [[baking tray]]\n| With a palette knife, spread the mixture out evenly onto the [[baking tray]]\n| In a [[Food processor|food processor]], mix the [[Cream cheese|cream cheese]], the remaining 2 [[Eggs|eggs]] and a teaspoons of [[Vanilla extract|vanilla extract]]\n| With the motor running, gradually add the [[Icing sugar|icing sugar]]\n| Pour this mixture over the top of the cake\n| [[Bake]] for 40 to 45 minutes then allow to cool\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nDust the top with a little extra [[Icing sugar|icing sugar]]\n===Chef's notes===\nNot surprisingly, the cake should be gooey under the crust!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#vanillaextract #gooeybuttercake #creamcheese #butter #icingsugar #bakingtray #yellowcakemix #freerangeeggs #eggs #egg #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->{{#seo:\n|title=Green chilli 'Tabasco' sauce - A Thermomix recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#indiangreenchillies #chillies #sauce #unusualrecipes #vinegar #tomatoes #fridge #tabasco #thermomix #seeds #scotch \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This Tabasco style sauce is made with Indian green chillies\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 233\n|PortionCalories = 233\n|DatePublished=29th July 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 1\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Green chilli 'Tabasco' sauce (TM) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Can't often buy Green Tabasco</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This is a close approximation</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[Tabasco]] style [[Sauce|sauce]] is made with [[Indian green chillies]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 600g [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], halved if small or quartered if larger\n| 200g [[Indian green chillies]], [[Seeds|seeds]] and skin retained, but stalk removed\n| 400g distilled white [[Vinegar|vinegar]]\n| 4 tbsps dark [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put all ingredients in the bowl, '''10 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 2''' \n| Then '''10 minutes / 100\u00b0C / Speed 2'''\n| Allow to cool a little, then '''1 minute / Speed 4-10 progressively'''\n| Pass through a [[Sieve|sieve]] and pour into a bottle or [[Lock & Lock]] tub.\n| Kept in the [[Fridge|fridge]], it will keep for a considerable time.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Very lightly adapted from Stef's recipe for '''[http://www.forumthermomix.com/index.php?topic=10345.0 Haba\u00f1ero Sauce Tabasco Style]''' on the '''[http://www.forumthermomix.com/index.php Thermomix Forum]'''\n===Variations===\nStef's recipe uses Haba\u00f1ero [[Chillies|chillies]], which I find are almost impossible to find in the UK as this time of year (July).  If you are lucky enough to obtain any (or [[Scotch]] Bonnets), you will find it hotter than making with [[Indian green chillies]].\n===Chef's notes===\nStef advises that you wear rubber gloves when you are preparing the [[Chillies|chillies]].  Also be careful of the fumes when removing the lid of the [[Thermomix]].\n===Servings===\nServings: 160 - About 800ml\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Pickles and preserves]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#indiangreenchillies #chillies #sauce #unusualrecipes #vinegar #tomatoes #fridge #tabasco #thermomix #seeds #scotch </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Hollywood Quesadillas, Vegetarian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheese #hollywoodquesadillas #diced #tortilla #salsa #pizza #quesadillas #peppers #jalapenos #tortillas #miseenplace \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I first had these when working next door (from a bar on Sunset Blvd. in 1979)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1605\n|PortionCalories = 802\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 2 as a snack\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 25 minutes (2 quesadillas)\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Hollywood Quesadillas recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Sound's fancy-pants</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Super tasty though</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nI first had these when working next door  (from a bar on Sunset Blvd. in 1979). The concept is simple, the ingredients simpler.I have enhanced the 'bar food' version, as I learned they could be more complete and more satisfying. Serve for snacks or a [[Light lunch|light lunch]]. Think of [[Quesadillas|quesadillas]] as [[Tex-Mex]] [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]] (10\"-12\")\n| 6 oz. [[Grated|grated]] [[Monterey Jack cheese]]\n| 1/3 cup fresh green or red [[Jalapeno|jalapeno]] [[Peppers|peppers]],  seeded and membraned, then [[Diced|diced]] fine\n| &frac12; cup [[Diced|diced]] [[Spanish]] (Yellow) [[Onion|onion]], fine diced\n| 3 tablespoons [[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]] ( or more) you choose the [[Salsa|salsa]]-I make my own)\n| Chopped [[Cilantro]] (opt.)\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]] (opt.)\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Have everything at or close to room temperature and a large [[Fry|fry]] pan!\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Spread all ingredients ( except [[Cheese|cheese]])with the back of a large spoon on [[Tortilla|tortilla]] one. Set [[Grill|grill]].hob to medium low..\n| Sprinkle [[Cheese|cheese]] over [[Tomato|tomato]] [[Pepper|pepper]] [[Salsa|salsa]]. Place second [[Tortilla|tortilla]] over top. slide this into the pan, and [[Steam|steam]] by using pan cover, or not if you want a more brittle version of [[Quesadillas|quesadillas]]. After about 5 minutes, flip the [[Quesadilla|quesadilla]] to [[Brown|brown]] tortilla 2. When it is all sizzling (3 minutes), transfer to cutting board and slice in [[Wedges|wedges]], as you would a [[Pizza|pizza]] or [[Cheesecake|cheesecake]], 3  or 4 to a plate.\n| This recipe can be multiplied for extra appetisers. Remember: you can put in refritos, [[Steamed|steamed]] [[Corn|corn]], chopped [[Olives|olives]]...but this is the core recipe.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a good light 'cervesa' ([[Beer|beer]]) and lots of paper towels\n===Variations===\nChange [[Cheeses|cheeses]]. Medium Cheddars, Canadian Brick [[Cheese]] or Colby  also work well. You can also use chopped jarred [[Jalapenos|jalapenos]] or others, but it isn't fresh anymore. Canned jalapenos are milder, usually, then their fresh ancestors.\n===Chef's notes===\nOnly the [[Tortillas|tortillas]], [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Cheese|cheese]] are constants.\n\nI found these difficult to flip, without emptying the contents all over the hob.  If you feel doubtful, use two plates to flip the quesadillas: Lay one over the pan, flip both over, place a second plate over the first, invert those, remove the top plate, replace with the pan, invert those, remove the plate.  ''If you can do a better job of explaining this, please do.''\n\nRecipe contributed by [[User:Tetramariner|Tetramariner]] 15:28, 30 January 2010 (GMT)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheese #hollywoodquesadillas #diced #tortilla #salsa #pizza #quesadillas #peppers #jalapenos #tortillas #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It's the [[masa harina]] that gives them that unique flavour.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &#189; cup of [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 1 pack of soft [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] (8 to 10 tortillas)\n| Fine [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut the each [[Corn tortillas|corn tortilla]] into 6 triangles\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large heavy based [[Frying pan|frying pan]] over a medium heat.\n| Add the triangles in small batches and [[Fry|fry]] for about a minute or until they just start to [[Brown|brown]].  You need to be quick as they can burn easily.\n| Lift the cooked [[Chips|chips]] out of the pan and let the [[Oil|oil]] drain and then stack on paper towels to remove excess oil.\n| Sprinkle with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]].\n| Allow to cool and crisp-up a little before serving.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTry one of our [[Salsa|salsa recipes]] or this [[Tex-Mex bean dip for tacos]].\n===Chef's notes===\nFor health reasons, I have used [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nYou could possibly fry the whole tortilla first and then cut into triangles as they remain soft for a ref minutes after frying.  I will try that next time I make these.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#corntortillas #homemadetortillachips #vegetableoil #chips #tortillachips #oliveoil #masaharina #panfried #corntortillarecipe #salsa #fry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Hoppin' John",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Hoppin' John recipe Cooking with chillies\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#hoppinjohn #peas #rice #bacon #hamhock #onion #boil #sausages #collardgreens #beans #simmer \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Hoppin' John is the Southern United States' version of the rice and beans dish traditional throughout the Caribbean\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4733\n|PortionCalories = 591\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 8\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Hoppin' John recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">No thanks</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I'd be hoppin' mad if someone served me this \ud83d\ude42</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Hoppin' John boil.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The rice is tender and the liquid is absorbed]]\n'''Hoppin' John''' is the Southern United States' version of the [[Rice|rice]] and [[Beans|beans]] dish traditional throughout the Caribbean. It consists of field [[Peas|peas]] or crowder peas ([[Black-eyed peas|black-eyed peas]]) and rice, with chopped [[Onion|onion]] and sliced [[Bacon|bacon]] or [[Sausages|sausages]], [[ham hock]] or fatback bacon.\n\nThroughout the coastal South, eating Hoppin' John on New Year's Day is thought to bring a year filled with luck, and it's eaten by everyone. The peas, or beans with little black \"eyes,\" signify coins. Fill your plate with them and your cup will run over, as in the 23rd Psalm, perhaps. [[Collard greens]] along with this dish are supposed to also add to the wealth since they are the colour of money. On the day after New Year's Day, leftover \"Hoppin' John\" is called '''\"Skippin' Jenny\"''', and further demonstrates one's frugality, bringing an even better chance of prosperity in the New Year, it is hoped.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 cups [[Dried|dried]] [[Black-eyed peas|black-eyed peas]] (about 340 g)\n| 2 cans of [[Black-eyed peas|black-eyed peas]], drained\n| 450 g (1 lb) lean slab [[Bacon|bacon]] \n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 1 small [[red bell pepper]], de-seeded and sliced\n| &#189; teaspoon crushed [[Chili flakes|chili flakes]]\n| &#189; teaspoon freshly ground [[cumin]] seeds\n| &#189; teaspoon dried [[oregano]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[sea salt]] or [[celery salt]]\n| 1 [[bay leaf]]\n| 4 cups water or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 2 cups uncooked long-[[Grain|grain]] white [[Rice|rice]]. [[Basmati rice]] is fine for this, though probably not authentic!\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If using canned black eyed [[Peas|peas]], start at step 5\n| Sort the [[Peas|peas]] and remove grit etc.\n| Soak in cold water, rinse and drain, repeat a few times\n| In a large pot, cover with cold water, bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 10 minutes, remove from heat and allow to stand for 2 hours.  Drain and rinse again.\n| To a large pot, add the soaked [[Black-eyed peas|black-eyed peas]], the [[ham hock]], the chopped [[Onion|onion]] and all of the herbs and spices.  If using spicy sausages I would wait for 1 hour before adding them\n| Add water or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Reduce the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 2 hours or until the [[Peas|peas]] are tender. (do not [[Boil|boil]] as the [[Beans|beans]] will burst)\n| Remove [[Bacon|bacon]], [[ham hock]] or [[Sausages|sausages]] and cut into bite-sized pieces\n| As with all [[rice]], rinse for a minute, in a sieve under cold running water to remove any excess starch\n| Return [[Meat|meat]] to pot. Stir in [[Rice|rice]], cover, and cook for 20 to 25 minutes or until rice is tender and liquid is absorbed\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n===Variations===\nTry 450 g (1 lb) meaty [[Ham hocks|ham hocks]] or 450 g (1 lb) thick spicy [[Sausage|sausage]] instead of the bacon.\n===Serving suggestion===\nServe with [[collard greens]], [[cornbread]] or fresh crusty bread.\n===Chef's note===\nIf you like a bit more gravy then reduce the amount of rice.  You could of course increase the amount of stock but you would need to adjust the seasoning as well.\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#hoppinjohn #peas #rice #bacon #hamhock #onion #boil #sausages #collardgreens #beans #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]

title": "Hot cheese and tomato hummus",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Hot cheese and tomato hummus recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#hummus #dried #oliveoil #hotcheeseandtomatohummus #refrigerated #vegetablestock #bean #chillisauce #driedblacklentils #butterbeans #lockandlock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A spicy bean pur\u00e9e based on a Mexican bean and cheese puree\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1591\n|PortionCalories = 397\n|DatePublished=17th August 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 17 hours\n |PrepTime = 12 hours 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 4 hours 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Hot cheese and tomato hummus.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Dipalicious!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The melted cheese on the top makes all the difference.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nNot really a [[hummus]], as I've not heard of a hot [[hummus]] before now. It's really a spicy [[bean]] [[pur\u00e9e]].  It's based on a [[Mexican bean and cheese puree]] and made with leftovers from the [[freezer]].  I added the sliced tomatoes to prevent the bean [[pur\u00e9e]] from drying out.\n\nA fantastic recipe and you would never imagine it was [[vegetarian]]!\n\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 90 g [[Dried|dried]] [[haricot beans]]\n| 90 g [[Dried|dried]] [[butter beans]]\n| 2 [[Litres|litres]] of weak [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] - I make up half the advised quantity of [[Bouillon|bouillon]] powder.\n| 2 sticks of [[celery]], roughly chopped\n| 1 large [[sweet pepper]], deseeded and chopped\n| 1 bulb of [[garlic]], peeled and crushed (''or to taste'')\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and roughly chopped\n| 3 tablespoons [[olive oil]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Tex-Mex seasoning]], or [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], or chopped [[chillies]], or [[chilli sauce]].\n| 110 g mature [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], roughly [[Grated|grated]].\n| 3 large tomatoes, thinly sliced\n| 1 to 2 tablespoons of yellow cornmeal.  Use '''only''' if the mixture looks far too wet and the end of the slow cooking process.\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n*  When you are ready to start the final bake, preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the beans in cold water overnight, rinsing and draining a few times if possible.\n| Add the soaked beans, stock, celery, peppers, garlic, chopped onion, Tex-Mex seasoning (or equivalent) to a [[slow cooker]] on low and cook for 4 hours\n| Using a [[stick blender]] reduce the mixture to the consistency of [[hummus]].  If it is really wet, add a tablespoon of [[yellow cornmeal]], stir well and check in another 15 minutes.  This is a very efficient way of reducing liquid, but use with caution as more than once, I've had to add more stock after doing this!\n| Add 1.5 tablespoons of olive oil.  Mix well and remove from the heat.\n| At this stage the mixture could be [[refrigerated]] or even [[frozen]] and the final cooking stage done at a later time.\n| Once the [[Oven|oven]] is hot, coat a [[shallow oven proof dish]] with 1.5 tablespoons of olive oil and spread the bean mixture evenly over the surface.\n| Sprinkle with grated [[cheese]] and top with the thinly sliced tomatoes.\n| [[Bake|bake]] the [[Puree|puree]] for about 45 minutes to 1 hour.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[soured cream]] and plain [[tortilla chips]] or broken up [[taco shells]] to use as edible spoons!\n\nThis dish is equally good hot or cold.  Store any unused [[pur\u00e9e]] in a [[Lock and Lock]] style box to prevent it drying out.\n===Chef's notes===\nI used [[dried black lentils]] for the beans and for health reasons, [[olive oil]] for the vegetable oil as this recipe uses rather a lot. For the cheese I used a mixture of mature [[gouda]] and mature [[cheddar]].\n\n===Variations===\nThis is a great recipe for experimentation.  Almost any vegetables can be added to this recipe.  Just use your imagination!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#hummus #dried #oliveoil #hotcheeseandtomatohummus #refrigerated #vegetablestock #bean #chillisauce #driedblacklentils #butterbeans #lockandlock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Masa harina fishcakes",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Masa harina fishcakes, Fish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#squash #masaharina #salmon #oliveoil #breadcrumbs #lemonjuice #chiliflakes #salmonfillets #masaharinafishcakes #onion #butter \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Another use for your garden squashes and pumpkins and an excuse to use your delicious masa harina. These freeze well too\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1038\n|PortionCalories = 173\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 6 - Makes about 12 fishcakes\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Salmon and pumpkin fishcakes recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Masa Harina makes the difference</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Such a special flavour; there is nothing quite like it.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nAnother use for your [[Garden squashes|garden squashes]] and [[Pumpkins|pumpkins]] and an excuse to use your delicious [[masa harina]].  These freeze well too.\n[[Image:Salmon and pumpkin fishcakes.jpg|thumb|300px|right|With extra prawns]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 small [[Squash|squash]] - about the size of a very large [[Grapefruit|grapefruit]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 2 fresh [[Salmon fillets|salmon fillets]]\n| 6 [[defrosted]] [[king prawns]], chopped small.\n| A little [[Milk|milk]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 medium [[onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| A handful of fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped\n| 2 teaspoons of [[chili flakes]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| 2 to 3 ladles of [[masa harina]] - I'm afraid I never got around to weighing the masa!\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]] beaten with a little [[Milk|milk]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 120 g [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[onion]] in a little [[olive oil]] until soft, about 5 minutes. Reserve.\n| Place the [[Salmon fillets|salmon fillets]] in a flat dish and add a little [[Milk|milk]] just so the [[Salmon|salmon]] stays moist.\n| Halve the [[Pumpkin|pumpkin]] and remove the [[Seeds|seeds]], leave the skin on as it's easier to remove the flesh after cooking than it is to peel first.\n| Cut a few slashes in the [[Squash|squash]], drizzle with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and season well\n| [[Roast]] in the top of the [[Oven|oven]] for 30 minutes or until the flesh is soft\n| After the [[Squash|squash]] has been [[Roasting|roasting]] for 15 minutes, [[Bake|bake]] the [[Salmon|salmon]], covered, in the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] for the last 15 minutes.\n| Scoop the [[Pumpkin|pumpkin]] flesh into a bowl, add the [[Butter|butter]], [[onions]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] seasoning and [[chili flakes]]. [[Mash|mash]] well.\n| Remove the skin from the [[Salmon|salmon]], drain and [[Flake|flake]] into the bowl with the [[Squash|squash]], add the [[masa harina]] and mix well.\n| Shape into oval patties, coat with beaten [[Egg|egg]] and roll in the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]. Refrigerate for 30 minutes to allow the [[masa harina]] to absorb the moisture.\n| Shallow [[Fry|fry]] for a few minutes a side turning often.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]] and [[Allioli a la moderna]] ([[Garlic mayonnaise|garlic mayonnaise]])\n===Variations===\nAdd [[Sesame seeds|sesame seeds]] to the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you don't want to use an [[Oven|oven]], the [[Squash|squash]] can be sliced and [[Boiled|boiled]] in water as you would [[Potatoes|potatoes]]. Leave the skin on for ease of preparation.  Half cover the [[Salmon|salmon]] with [[Milk|milk]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] in a shallow pan for 6 minutes, turning once.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#squash #masaharina #salmon #oliveoil #breadcrumbs #lemonjuice #chiliflakes #salmonfillets #masaharinafishcakes #onion #butter </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

title": "Memphis BBQ pulled duck tacos",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Memphis BBQ pulled duck tacos recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#duck #memphisbbqpulledducktacos #barbecuesauce #tacotrays #tacos #tacoshells #springonions #sourcream #sauce #fat #cherries \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Crispy tacos filled with Gressingham pulled duck and salad, serve with sour cream and black cherries\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1008\n|PortionCalories = 504\n|DatePublished=30th November 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  35 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Memphis BBQ pulled duck tacos recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice, but...</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">What an expensive way to buy duck! \ud83e\udd2d</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe is more an assembly list than a recipe.  I spotted the [[Gressingham Memphis Barbecue Pulled Duck]] in Morrisons and thought it would make a good [[Taco|taco]] filling. \n\nThe [[Duck|duck]] was very good and I'll be getting more today.  Do note though that the duck is notreally pulled duck, it's duck legs with a sauce that need to be ''pulled'' once they've been cooked.  \n\nThe Old El Paso [[Tacos|tacos]] however, ''really'' let this recipe down.  They are so thin now that they break apart as you touch them. Any because they are so miserably thin, they don't even have the crunch purported on the packet.  Another cynical attempt at increasing profits I guess.\n\nIf you don't want to use the flimsy El Paso [[Tacos]], try to hunt down the cheaper and far nice Discovery [[Taco trays|taco trays]], or forget tacos altogether and use [[Corn|corn]] or [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]] instead.\n\nThe [[Duck|duck]] feels like it might serve 4 but is actually contains 2 duck legs, a [[Foil|foil]] tray and a sachet of [[Sauce|sauce]], plenty for 2 people, not enough for four.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 pack [[Gressingham Memphis BBQ Pulled Duck]] (2 duck legs in with [[Barbecue sauce|barbecue sauce]])\n| 1 Pack Discovery [[Taco trays|taco trays]] or if you must ,1 Pack El Paso [[Taco shells]] (see notes above)\n| 6 [[Spring onions|spring onions]]\n| 12 [[Baby tomatoes|baby tomatoes]]\n| Half a green [[Sweet Pepper|sweet pepper]]\n| 10 [[Black cherries|black cherries]]\n| 150 ml pot of [[Sour cream|sour cream]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Memphis BBQ pulled duck tacos ingredients.jpg|thumb|right|300px|The basic ingredients\nImage:Gressingham Memphis Barbecue Pulled Duck.jpg|thumb|right|300px|[[Gressingham Memphis Barbecue Pulled Duck]] (whole duck legs with sauce)\n</gallery>\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Remove the [[Duck|duck]] legs from the plastic wrapping and place in the tray provided, make sure you include all the lovely [[Fat|fat]] too!\n| Leave the [[Sauce|sauce]] sachet to one side for now\n| [[Roast]] the [[Duck|duck]] legs at 180\u00b0 C for 25 minutes, uncovered, in the tray provided\n| After 25 minutes, drain and discard some of the cooking juices (see [[Chef's notes]] below).\n| Add the contents of the Memphis [[Barbecue sauce|barbecue sauce]] to the duck's legs and mix well\n| [[Bake]] for a further 10 minutes\n| When there is 5 minutes remaining pop the [[Taco trays|taco trays]] or fragile El Paso [[Taco shells|taco shells]] into the [[Oven|oven]] to warm up\n| Meanwhile: chop the [[Spring onions|spring onions]] ([[Scallions|scallions]])\n| Halve the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| Halve the [[Cherries|cherries]] and remove the stones\n| Chop the [[Green pepper|green pepper]]\n| Using two forks, shred the [[Duck|duck]] legs with two forks\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the pulled [[Duck|duck]], [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and [[Tacos|tacos]] and [[Sour cream|sour cream]] in separate dishes so diners can assemble the tacos at the table\n===Variations===\nUse whatever filling ingredients that take your fancy, some other suggestions, sliced red onions, avocado, pickled chillies, crispy lettuce, pineapple chunks.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Gressingham BBQ Pulled Duck]] (legs) are already pre-cooked. If you are using [[Fresh duck|fresh duck]] legs, they will will probably take about the same time, but the [[Oven|oven]] could do with being 1 little warmed (190\u00b0 C - 200\u00b0 C) and they will benefit from resting for 15 minutes once removed from the oven.\n\nThe cooking instructions on the [[Gressingham Pulled Duck]] suggests discarding all of the cooking juices after 25 minutes of [[Roasting|roasting]]. I would definitely suggest otherwise.  Next time I will mix them in with the [[Barbecue sauce|barbecue sauce]], and not waste them.\n\nI allowed the juices to solidify overnight and it was almost all lovely tasty jelly, hardly any [[Fat|fat]] - made a great [[Sandwich|sandwich]] filling and reminded me of jelly and [[Dripping|dripping]] of old.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#duck #memphisbbqpulledducktacos #barbecuesauce #tacotrays #tacos #tacoshells #springonions #sourcream #sauce #fat #cherries </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Mexican bean and cheese puree",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mexican bean and cheese puree a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beans #mexicanbeanandcheesepuree #oliveoil #simmer #grated #bean #stock #chillies #tabascosauce #mexican #mexico \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Based on a recipe from my cookbook of the moment: Diana Kennedy's wonderful Mexican cookbook, Essential cuisines of Mexico\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2347\n|PortionCalories = 586\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 to 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 15 hours\n |PrepTime = 12 hours 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 2 hours 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mexican bean and cheese puree recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow! I remember this</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This was great and it's veggie!</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nBased on a recipe from my cookbook of the moment: Diana Kennedy's wonderful [[Mexican]] cookbook, ''Essential cuisines of [[Mexico]]'' ISBN 9780307587725, this Mexican baked bean recipe would make a great side dish, a snack-style lunch dip for crispy tortilla chips or even a main course.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 180 g [[Dried|dried]] [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]]\n| 2 [[Litres|litres]] of weak [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| &#189; a small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and roughly chopped\n| 1.5 tablespoons [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 100 ml [[olive oil]]\n| 1/2 to 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 110 ml full [[Cream|cream]] [[Milk|milk]]\n| 3 [[Ancho chillies|ancho chillies]], rehydrated and deseeded\n| 110 g strong [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], roughly [[Grated|grated]].\n| Freshly ground [[black pepper]] and [[Tabasco sauce]] to taste\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n*  Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the beans in cold water overnight, rinsing and draining a few times if possible.\n| Cover the beans with twice the volume of cold water, bring to the boil and simmer uncovered for 30 minutes.  Skim any scum that appears on the surface.\n| Drain the beans and return to the pan. Pour 1.5 tablespoons of [[Oil|oil]] over the beans, add the onion pieces and the stock. Bring to the boil, cover and reduce to a simmer.\n| [[Simmer]] for about 30 minutes or until they are softening and the skins beginning to [[Split|split]].\n| Add the 100 ml of olive oil to a [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]] and place in the oven whilst it is preheating.\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]] and continue to [[Simmer|simmer]] for another 35 minutes until the [[Beans|beans]] become a mush.  this time will very depending upon the type of bean.\n| If they dry out during this stage add a little more [[Stock|stock]].\n| Remove the [[Beans|beans]] from the heat, drain them and using a [[Food processor|food processor]], blend them to a pur\u00e9e with the [[Milk|milk]] and [[chillies]].\n| Taste for seasoning and add [[Tabasco sauce]] to taste if using.\n| Once the [[Oven|oven]] is hot, carefully stir the [[Bean|bean]] pur\u00e9e into the hot [[Oil|oil]] and mix very well.  Don't be concerned about the obvious amount of excess oil, this will absorb into the bean mixture during the last 15 minutes of cooking. \n| Return the [[Casserole|casserole]] of [[Beans|beans]] to the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Bake|bake]] the [[Puree|puree]] for about 45 minutes to 1 hour.\n| By now the [[Beans|beans]] should be [[Drying|drying]] out at the edges, don't add any more [[Stock|stock]] at this stage.\n| Sprinkle the [[Beans|beans]] with the [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]] and return to the [[Oven|oven]] for 15 minutes or until melted.\n| Serve directly.\n}}\n===Variations===\nI like to fiddle with my recipes and encouraged by the recent success [[Dal makhani]], I also added 3 fat crushed cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] and 200 ml of chopped tomatoes at the blending stage.\n\n[[Dried|dried]] [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]], [[chick peas]] or any similar dried [[Bean|bean]] work fine in this recipe.\n\nI think that [[yogurt]] would work just as well as [[milk]] too.\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[soured cream]] and plain [[tortilla chips]] to use as edible spoons!\n===Chef's notes===\nI used [[dried black lentils]] for the beans and for health reasons, [[olive oil]] for the vegetable oil as this recipe uses rather a lot. For the cheese I used a mixture of mature [[gouda]] and mature [[cheddar]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beans #mexicanbeanandcheesepuree #oliveoil #simmer #grated #bean #stock #chillies #tabascosauce #mexican #mexico </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
