Good with [[grilled]] [[fish]] as well as grilled [[chicken]] or [[pork]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 675 g (1&frac12; lb) [[sweet potatoes]] \n| 1/2 a teaspoon of crushed [[dried]] chilies\n| 4 [[spring onions]], finely chopped\n| Juice of &frac34; of an [[orange]]\n| Juice of &frac34; of a small [[lime]]\n| Finely chopped [[zest]] from &frac14; of a [[lime]]\n| Pinch of [[sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Peel the [[sweet potatoes]] and dice to 1 cm (&frac12;\") cubes\n| Add the cubes to a pan of boiling water and [[boil]] for 10 minutes\n| Drain and return to the pan for another 5 minutes, covered but unheated, to allow the [[potatoes]] to dry out\n| Add the [[dried]] [[sweet potatoes]] to a serving bowl and chill in the refrigerator for 20 minutes\n| Mix the [[orange]], [[lime juice]], crushed [[chillies]] and [[spring onions]] together\n| When ready to serve, toss the [[sweet potatoes]] in the juice mix, season with [[sea salt]] and serve\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sweetpotatoes #sweetpotatosalsa #lime #orange #springonions #dried #potatoes #pork #sidedish #chicken #boiledorsimmered </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Order them online or visit the fabulous food market.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 825g La Coste\u00f1a Tender Cactus Nopalitos (1 Jar)\n| &#189; [[Cup|cup]] of thin sliced or finely chopped [[Red onion|red onion]]\n| 3 medium [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] seeded and chopped\n| &#188; [[Cup|cup]] finely chopped [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] (more if you like)\n| &#189; tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Juice]] of 1 fresh [[Lime|lime]]\n| &#188; teaspoon dried [[Mexican oregano]]\n| 1-2 La Coste\u00f1a [[Jalape\u00f1os]] Chilies, finely chopped (optional)\n| 1 [[Cup]] [[La Coste\u00f1a Refried Pinto beans]] \n| 75g [[Shredded]] [[Cheese|cheese]] ([[mozzarella]], [[Cheddar|cheddar]], [[Halloumi|halloumi]]) (optional)\n| 8 [[Corn tortillas]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Drain La Coste\u00f1a nopalitos.\n| Place the [[nopalitos]] in a [[Salad|salad]] bowl and add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Chilies|chilies]].\n| Whisk together the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], [[Oregano|oregano]] and pour all over. Toss to [[Blend|blend]] well.\n| Heat La Coste\u00f1a Refried beans on a [[Stove|stove]] or in [[Microwave|microwave]].\n| Heat [[Tortillas|tortillas]] on a flat pan then wrap in a [[Kitchen towel|kitchen towel]] to keep them warm.\n| Place them inside a bamboo [[Steamer|steamer]] or any other plastic container with lid.\n| Place about 2 tablespoons of [[La Costena Refried beans]] on the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] and top with another 2 tablespoons of the [[Vegetable|vegetable]] mixture.\n| Top with some [[Cheese|cheese]] if you like.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:MexTrade.co.uk recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Steamed]]\n===Recipe source===\n{{Template:RecipeCourtesyOfMexTrade.co.uk}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cup #tomatoes #oliveoil #cheese #shredded #cheddar #kitchentowel #tendercactus #mozzarella #mexicanfood #corianderleaves </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Tex-Mex beercan chicken",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tex-Mex beercan chicken, a chicken recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beer #chicken #texmexbeercanchicken #tacomix #oliveoil #wine #cider #cocktailstick #roastpotatoes #steam #orange \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is an unusual way to cook chicken with beer\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2711\n|PortionCalories = 677\n|DatePublished=28th July 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Tex-Mex beercan chicken recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">You MUST make this</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This was one of the first 'variations' on beer can chicken that I ever made, and it's once of the best.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is an unusual way to cook [[Chicken|chicken]] with [[beer]]. The basic idea is to carefully balance the chicken on a 3/4 full can of beer using its legs as an additional support, coat it with a flavoured rub and [[roast]] it.  The [[Steam|steam]] from the beer permeates the chicken to produce a succulent dish.  I think my [[Taco mix|taco mix]] suits this admirably, though any flavoured rub would do.\n\nOur American friends seem to barbecue chicken using this method, and though I'm sure it's worth trying, I can't believe that the upper part of the chicken would even get warm on our barbecue.  And we have a BIG barbecue.  I would welcome any feedback.\n\nThe process is made even easier and safer with one of these: [[Grillpro Stainless Steel Chicken Roaster]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.5kg free range [[Chicken|chicken]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[Taco mix|taco mix]], El Paso taco mix or a seasoning rub of your choice\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 440ml can of [[Beer|beer]] or [[Lager|lager]] \n| 1 [[tangerine]] or [[orange]] (optional)\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - Gas 6)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Wash the outside of the beer can\n| [[Parson's nose|Remove the parson's nose]], any giblets, bags, tranklements etc. from the [[Chicken|chicken]] \n| Cut off and discard the [[Parson's nose]].\n| Rinse inside and out under cold running water and pat dry with kitchen towel\n| Rub 1 tablespoon of the [[Taco mix|taco mix]] into the cavity of the bird \n| Rub the outside of the [[Chicken|chicken]] with the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and coat with 3 tablespoons of [[Taco mix|taco mix]]\n| Seal the neck of the bird by folding over and skewering with [[skewers]] or [[cocktail sticks]] \n| Open the [[Beer|beer]] and toast the start of the proceedings with about a &#188; of the beer - you don't want a full can\n| Punch a few holes around the empty top-part of the can\n| Add the remaining rub to the [[Beer|beer]] tin\n| Sit the [[Chicken|chicken]] on the [[Beer|beer]] can in a baking tray and balance it on its legs. A small chicken sits quite happily; a large chicken might be a bit trickier\n| Cut the top off the tangerine so the juice can run down while it cooks, affix with a [[cocktail stick]] into the top cavity (see photo) and add the cut slice as a hat!\n| Place the baking tray in the bottom of the oven\n| After 30 minutes, reduce the heat to 180\u00b0 C ( 350\u00b0 F - Gas 4)\n| The [[Chicken|chicken]] should be cooked in about 1.5 hours [total cooking timw], depending upon the size of the bird. Check every 15 minutes towards the end.  It is done when the juices run clear if the deepest part of the flesh (eg the thigh) is pierced with a metal skewer or sharp knife\n| Remove the [[Chicken|chicken]] extremely carefully with [[Oven gloves|oven gloves]] and tongs if needed.\n| Allow to rest for 10 minutes before carving\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Tex-Mex beercan chicken ready.jpg|thumb|250px|right|Oven-ready!\nImage:Tex-Mex beercan chicken ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The basic ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nUsing [[The Jamie Oliver carving method|the Jamie Oliver carving method]], serve with [[roast potatoes]] and [[garlic mayonnaise]].\n\nThe remaining beer could be used to make gravy if needed.\n===Variations===\nTry this with a cock [[pheasant]] (hens are too small) and use [[cider]] or [[wine]] instead of [[beer]].  Wash out an empty 440 ml [[beer]] can and pour 330 ml of dry white [[wine]] or dry [[cider]] into it.  For this, a [[herb]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] rub is excellent - this can be made with the ingredients (minus the [[onion]] and [[pork]]) used in the [[Slow roast herby pork belly]] recipe.\n\nWe have also tried this with a small [[duck]], but the cavity was too large for the [[beer]] can, but not big enough for two cans.  Duckling might be worth a try if you can get it.\n===Chicken falls over?===\nMy chicken has just fallen over, I may have to get one of these: [http://www.socal.co.uk/BBQ_Accessories/Beer_Can_Chicken/Grillpro_Stainless_Steel_Chicken_Roaster/332/17302 (beer can) Chicken roaster]\n\nLarge chickens seem to be ok - it's the smaller birds that have problems balancing on a beer can.  440ml is probably the biggest can you should use with all but the largest birds. The last few times I have made this, I have placed the chicken and can inside an oven proof saucepan, in the oven, so the chicken has a little more support if it tends to lean over.  It also makes far less mess if it does fall over!\n\n... or go for the real thing: '''[[Grillpro Stainless Steel Chicken Roaster]]'''!\n{{Template:Beercan chicken - See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Cooking with beer|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beer #chicken #texmexbeercanchicken #tacomix #oliveoil #wine #cider #cocktailstick #roastpotatoes #steam #orange </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

I make my own Tex-Mex mix / Taco mix but you can buy it in packet form in most supermarkets\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1280\n|PortionCalories = 640\n|DatePublished=30th June 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Accompanied by [[Spicy honey glazed butternut squash]] and [[broccoli]]\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  5 minutes\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Spicy honeyglazed butternut squash recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">The spice makes the difference.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The livens-up an average pork chop, and makes an exceptional one brilliant.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nA really simple recipe that livens up [[Pork chops|pork chops]].\n[[Image:Old El Paso Taco Mix.jpg|thumb|200px|right|Old El Paso Taco Mix, the BIG container!]]\n\nI make my own [[Taco mix|Tex-Mex mix / Taco mix]] but you can buy it in packet form in most supermarkets. I found [[Old India Taco Seasoning]] and was very pleased with the results.\n\nI cooked these in the [[Oven|oven]] as it was already on for the [[Spicy honey-glazed butternut squash]].  It also uses less [[Fat|fat]] this way.  You could just as easily [[Grill|grill]] or [[Fry|fry]] these.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 [[Pork chops|pork chops]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Ground|ground]] [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]]\n| 1 beaten [[Egg|egg]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Tex-Mex mix|Taco mix]], or to taste\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Mix the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]], [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]] and [[Tex-Mex]] mix together and spread out on a plate\n| [[Dip]] the [[Pork chops|pork chops]] in the beaten [[Egg|egg]], then coat the [[Pork chops|pork chops]] with the spicy [[Breadcrumb|breadcrumb]] mix\n| Place on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] with a wire grid and [[Bake|bake]] for 25 minutes.\n| Check that the [[Pork|pork]] is properly cooked, allow to [[Rest for|rest for]] 5 minutes, then serve.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#porkchops #texmexbreadedporkchops #cornmeal #breadcrumbs #egg #barbecued #grill #breadcrumb #pork #fry #ground </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tex-Mex breaded smoked salmon recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#masaharina #salmon #egg #plainflour #breadcrumbs #smokedsalmon #tacoseasoning #breadcrumb #oliveoil #salads #spices \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=We had a packet of thinly sliced smoked salmon leftover from Christmas so I thought rather than eating it raw, I would find a different way to serve it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 605\n|PortionCalories = 302\n|DatePublished=5th January 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:TexMex breaded smoked salmon recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Again, again? \ud83e\udd17</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">So I ask, what's not to like?</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nWe had a packet of thinly sliced [[Smoked|smoked]]  [[Salmon|salmon]] leftover from Christmas so I thought rather than eating it raw, I would find a way to cook it for a change.\n[[Image:TexMex breaded smoked salmon prep.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The breading production line!]]\n\nI used [[Old India Taco Seasoning]] for the [[Spices|spices]] and [[Masa Harina|masa harina]] where I would normally use [[Plain flour|plain flour]].  If you don't have the Old [[India]] [[Taco seasoning|taco seasoning]] you could use homemade [[Tex-Mex seasoning]], a different [[Taco|taco]] seasoning or your own [[Blend|blend]] of spices.  This was so good, we're having again tonight!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 125g packet of thinly sliced [[Smoked salmon|smoked salmon]]\n| 1 beaten [[Egg|egg]]\n| 5 tablespoons [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Old India Taco Seasoning]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Masa Harina|masa harina]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Separate the [[Smoked salmon|smoked salmon]] sheets and cut them smaller if they are very large.\n| Add the [[Old India Taco Seasoning]] to the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and mix well.  Tip this mix onto a large plate.\n| Add the [[Masa Harina|masa harina]] to one plate and the beaten [[Egg|egg]] to another.\n| Put 3 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] into a large pan and heat gently.\n| Dredge each [[Salmon|salmon]] sheet in [[Masa Harina|masa harina]] (or [[Plain flour|plain flour]]), [[Dip|dip]] it in the beaten [[Egg|egg]] to coat both sides then dredge it through the [[Breadcrumb|breadcrumb]] mix, patting it down to ensure a good covering.\n| Pop the coated [[Salmon|salmon]] into the pan and cook for 2 minutes a side, turning once.  You may need to do this in batches rather than crowding the pan.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a selection of [[Salads|salads]].\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you are using [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], don't add any extra salt as the mix is already quite salty.  If you add extra seasoning, it won't get any spicier, it will just get saltier.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#masaharina #salmon #egg #plainflour #breadcrumbs #smokedsalmon #tacoseasoning #breadcrumb #oliveoil #salads #spices </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

-->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 700\n|PortionCalories = 175\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Fried, spicy and crunchy\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 2 hours 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 2 hours\n|CookTime = 20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Tex-Mex pork fried.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Spicy fried pork</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Perfect with chips \ud83d\udc37\ud83c\udf5f\ud83d\udc37\ud83c\udf5f\ud83d\udc37\ud83c\udf5f. </span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nTry this [[Pork|pork]] recipe for [[Mexican]]-style [[Fried|fried]] pork, using the best cut of pork and your favourite [[Chillies|chillies]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[Pork|pork]] fillet cut into 4 steaks or 4 pork escallops, [[Pork fillet|flattened as shown here]] (don't cut them into strips though)\n| 1 tablespoon [[Cider|cider]] [[Vinegar|vinegar]]\n| 2 of your favourite [[Chillies|chillies]], rehydrated if dried and deseeded (to taste)\n| 2 [[Cloves|cloves]] of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| Sea [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Juice of 1 [[lemon]]\n| Dash of [[olive oil]] for the marinade\n| [[Olive]] [[Oil|oil]] for fryng (It's not authentic, but I feel so much healthier when [[Frying|frying]] with [[Olive oil|olive oil]]!)\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]], beaten\n}}\n\n'''Seasoned [[Flour|flour]]'''\n* Sea [[Salt|salt]] and freshly ground [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n* 75 g (3 oz ) [[masa harina]] or [[yellow cornmeal]]\n* 75 g (3 oz ) plain [[Flour|flour]]\n* 2 tablespoons of [[Taco mix]]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix together, the [[Vinegar|vinegar]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]], [[lemon juice]] and a splash of [[olive oil]] and mix to a thin marinade.\n| Coat the [[Pork|pork]] steaks with the marinade, refrigerate and allow to infuse for at least 2 hours.\n| Add the two flours, the [[taco mix]] to a shallow dish and mix well to combine\n|# You can omit the taco mix but it would be a shame as it gives the coating a homemade 'Kentucky-fried' flavour.\n| [[Dip]] both sides of the steaks into the seasoned [[Flour|flour]]\n| Knock off any excess [[Flour|flour]] and [[Dip|dip]] into the beaten [[Egg|egg]], then back into the seasoned flour.\n| Again, knock off any excess [[Flour|flour]].\n| [[Fry]] in a little [[Olive|olive]] [[Oil|oil]] until the pork is properly cooked and golden brown on both sides.\n| Pat any excess [[Oil|oil]] off on a kitchen towel.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Pork fillet breaded.jpg|thumb|300px|right|'Breaded' fillets\nImage:Pork fillet marinade.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Marinading\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with [[yellow rice]] and [[tomato salsa]].\n\n===Chef's note===\n\nIf you can't get [[Masa harina]] then use [[yellow cornmeal]] instead.\n\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pork]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pork]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Pork]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Pork]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Pork]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#flour #chillies #pork #oliveoil #egg #garlic #blackpepper #olive #dip #masaharina #yellowcornmeal </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Using a medium chicken and lots of home made salsa it would probably stretch to 6 people.  I added crushed new potatoes to the wrap, just because we had some spare - that helped to bulk it out and made it a little different.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 1 teaspoon white [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]] [[Ground|ground]] to powder\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] (or to taste)\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Garlic powder|garlic powder]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Ginger powder|ginger powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Coriander seeds|coriander seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] to powder\n| 1 teaspoon of [[paprika powder]], [[smoked paprika powder]] is even better if you have it.\n| Pinch of [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]] powder\n|* Note to self: go easy on the [[cinnamon]]!\n| 1kg [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces for four people, skin removed - one medium 1.3kg [[chicken, jointed]], is ideal.\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n| 2 teaspoons of [[muscovado sugar]] or [[brown sugar]]\n| 190 ml (3/4 cup) cup of [[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]], you can make your own here but bottled [[Salsa|salsa]] is still pretty good\n| 250 ml (1 cup) [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| [[Juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of &#189; a [[Lime|lime]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a pan and gently saut\u00e9 the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] until it is translucent - about 6 minutes\n| Add the [[Spices|spices]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for a few minutes\n| Mix in the [[Chicken|chicken]], [[Salsa|salsa]] [[brown sugar]] and [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]], bring to the [[Boil|boil]] then reduce to a [[Simmer|simmer]]\n| Cover and cook for 40 minutes then remove the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces from the pot and allow to cool a little\n| Leave the cover off the pan and continue [[Simmering|simmering]] the [[Sauce|sauce]] until it is reduced by more than half and most of the sauce has gone - probably another 30 minutes.\n| Meanwhile use 2 forks and shred the [[Meat|meat]] from the [[bones]]\n| Once the [[Sauce|sauce]] has reduced, add back the [[Chicken|chicken]], mix in the [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] and season to taste\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Tex-Mex pulled chicken reduced.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Pulled chicken - after reducing the sauce and adding back the shredded chicken\nImage:Tex-Mex pulled chicken sauce.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The sauce after about 20 minutes\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe on [[Tortillas|tortillas]] or similar [[Flat breads|flat breads]]\nGarnish with [[Avocado|avocado]] slices, slices of lime, [[Soured cream|soured cream]] and salad leaves\n===Variations===\nThis makes a great [[Sandwich|sandwich]] filler too.\n===Chef's notes===\nAs I almost invariably do after jointing a chicken, I cut slashes all over the chicken pieces; refrigerate and marinade them in the juice of a lime and a big pinch of salt.  It's a habit picked up from an Indian cookery course that seems to make chicken very tender and tasty.\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]][[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#texmexpulledchicken #chicken #brownsugar #garlic #sauce #onion #oliveoil #ground #salsa #zest #chickenstock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tex-Mex seasoning recipe Cooking with chillies\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#texmexseasoning #chilipowder #oregano #vegetableoil #paprikapowder #whitecumin #stock #driedgarlicgranules #garlic #coffeegrinder #beef \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Rather than buying packets of Mexican spice mix from that well known company, make your own. It's easy, allows you to tailor it to your taste\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 35\n|PortionCalories = 35\n|DatePublished=22nd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = 8 teaspoons of the spice mix is the equivalent of a 35 g (1.25 oz) packet of [[taco]] seasoning\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Tex-Mex seasoning recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Better than El Paso mixes</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This beats the (expensive) commercially made Tex Mex mixes, hands down.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nRather than buying packets of Mexican spice mix from that well known company, make your own.  It's easy, allows you to tailor it to your taste.  The recipe is easy to adjust to make different quantities.\n\nThe Main ingredients that give that authentic flavour are the [[oregano]], [[cumin seeds]] and [[chili powder]].  I would suggest you keep those at the levels here and adjust the other items if you have a desire to tinker.\n\nEverything is in teaspoons to make it easy to make different quantities - use tablespoons at the same rate to make more.\n===Commercially available Tex-Mex seasoning===\nI also use ready made seasoning mixes, but the one I had been using changed and was far too salty so I went in search of another supplier.  This let to my discovery of [[Taste Sensation Ltd]].  if you love your spices and seasonings, take a look at them.  They sell them directly and via [https://www.amazon.co.uk/stores/TasteSensation/node/4434351031 Amazon UK] and I can thoroughly recommend them.  Also, Nick Lumby, who has run the company for 20 years, is a really nice guy!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 teaspoons [[chili powder]] or chili flakes or crushed dried chillies\n| 2 teaspoons [[paprika powder]]\n| 2 teaspoons dried [[Mexican oregano]] or [[oregano]] leaves\n| 3 teaspoons [[dried garlic granules]] or [[Garlic|garlic]] powder\n| 1 teaspoon [[sea salt]]\n| 6 teaspoons [[white cumin]] seeds\n| 5 teaspoons [[onion]] powder or dried onion flakes\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Grind all the ingredients to powder in a [[coffee grinder]]\n| Mix together well if you had to do this in batches\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\n\nStore in an airtight container out of the light.\n\n35 g of this spice mix is sufficient to season; [[chicken]], [[pork]], [[beef]] for four people.  Rub the mix on the [[meat]], coat well with a tablespoon of [[vegetable oil]] and 1 tablespoon [[lemon juice]] and marinate for 2 hours.\n\nI've recently discovered [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], which saves me from makling this.  It's sold in 500g quantities, which last us about 4 months!  Wonderful stuff.  Give it a try.\n\nA good [[:Category:Indian ingredients (supplier)|Asian grocer / wholesaler]] will [[stock]] all of the ingredients for this recipe, and a whole lot more besides!\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Spices]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#texmexseasoning #chilipowder #oregano #vegetableoil #paprikapowder #whitecumin #stock #driedgarlicgranules #garlic #coffeegrinder #beef </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

#simmer #molasses \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a 1st place winner in an annual North Texas Chili Cook off\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 5072\n|PortionCalories = 634\n|DatePublished=29th March 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Big Tex, mascot of the State Fair of Texas\n|Servings = Serves 8\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  2 hours, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  30 minutes\n|CookTime =  2 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Big Tex.JPG|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Definately a winner</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Y9ou can taste the different chillies in this too.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a 1st place winner in an annual North Texas Chili Cook off.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 6 [[Dried|dried]] [[Ancho]] [[Chile peppers|chile peppers]] (about 1 \u00be ounces), stems and [[Seeds|seeds]] removed, and flesh torn into 1-inch pieces \n| 2 [[Dried|dried]] Arbol [[Chile peppers|chile peppers]], stems removed, pods [[Split|split]], [[Seeds|seeds]] removed \n| 3 tablespoons [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| 2 teaspoons unsweetened [[Cocoa powder|cocoa powder]]\n| 2.5 cups low-[[Sodium|sodium]] [[Chicken|chicken]] [[Broth|broth]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], cut into 3/4-inch pieces (about 2 cups) \n| 3 small [[Jalapeno]] [[Chilies|chilies]], stems and [[Seeds|seeds]] removed and discarded, flesh cut into \u00bd-inch pieces\n| 4 medium [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Cloves|cloves]], [[Minced|minced]] or pressed through [[Garlic press|garlic press]] (about 4 teaspoons)\n| 2 (14 \u00bd ounce) can [[Diced|diced]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 50ml [[Tomato paste|tomato paste]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 2 teaspoons light [[Molasses|molasses]]\n| 4.5 pounds blade steaks, trimmed of gristle and [[Fat|fat]] and cut into \u00be-inch pieces \n| 1 (12 ounce) bottle [[Lager|lager]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\nPreheat the oven to 150\u00b0 C (300\u00b0 F - gas 2), [fan oven 130\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Place [[Ancho]] [[Chilies|chilies]] in 12-inch [[Skillet|skillet]] over medium-high heat; toast, stirring frequently, until flesh is dry and fragrant, 4-6 minutes, reducing heat if [[Chilies|chilies]] begin to smoke. \n| Transfer to bowl of [[Food processor|food processor]] and cool. Do not wash out [[Skillet|skillet]].\n| Add Arbol [[Chilies|chilies]], [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]], [[Oregano|oregano]], [[Cumin|cumin]], [[Cocoa|cocoa]], and 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]] to [[Food processor|food processor]] with [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Ancho]] [[Chilies|chilies]]; process until finely [[Ground|ground]], about 2 minutes. With processor running, very slowly add \u00bd cup [[Broth|broth]] until smooth, thick paste forms, about 45 seconds, scraping down sides of bowl as necessary. Transfer to small bowl. Place [[Onions|onions]] in now-empty processor bowl and pulse until roughly chopped, about four 1-second [[Pulses|pulses]]. Add [[Jalapenos|jalapenos]] and pulse until consistency of chunky [[Salsa|salsa]], about four 1-second [[Pulses|pulses]], scraping down bowl as necessary.\n| Heat 1 tablespoon [[Oil|oil]] in large [[Dutch Oven|dutch oven]] over medium-high heat. Add [[Onion|onion]] mixture and cook, stirring occasionally, until any exuded moisture has evaporated and [[Vegetables|vegetables]] are softened, 7 to 9 minutes. Add [[Garlic|garlic]] and cook until fragrant, about 1 minute. Add [[Chili|chili]] paste, [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Tomato paste|tomato paste]], [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Molasses|molasses]]; stir until [[Chili|chili]] paste is thoroughly combined. Add remaining 2 cups [[Broth|broth]]; bring to [[Boil|boil]] then reduce heat to [[Simmer|simmer]].\n| Meanwhile, heat 1 tablespoon [[Oil|oil]] in 12-inch [[Skillet|skillet]] over medium-high heat. Pat [[Beef|beef]] dry with [[Paper towels|paper towels]] and sprinkle with 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]. Add half of [[Beef|beef]] and cook until [[Browned|browned]] on all sides, about 8 minutes. Transfer [[Meat|meat]] to [[Dutch Oven|dutch oven]]. Add \u00bd bottle [[Lager|lager]] to [[Skillet|skillet]], scraping bottom of pan to loosen any [[Browned|browned]] bits, and bring to [[Simmer|simmer]]. Transfer [[Lager|lager]] to [[Dutch oven]]. Repeat with remaining [[Oil|oil]], beef, and lager. Once last addition of lager has been added to [[Dutch Oven|dutch oven]], stir to combine and return mixture to [[Simmer|simmer]]. \n| Cover pot and transfer to [[Oven|oven]]. Cook until [[Meat|meat]] is fully tender, 1 \u00bd to 2 hours. Let [[Chili|chili]] stand, uncovered, for 10 minutes. Stir well and season to taste with [[Salt|salt]].\n}}\n===See also===\n* {{ChiliConCarne}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with beer]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chilies #dutchoven #skillet #texaschili #lager #broth #chili #seeds #ancho #simmer #molasses </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Lupita is a true reflection of the incredible flavours, colours and aromas found throughout Mexico City.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 500 g cooked [[Shredded|shredded]] [[Beef|beef]] brisket\n| 700 g [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]]\n| 200 g of La Coste\u00f1a green tomatillo\n| 150 g of La Coste\u00f1a Chile Chipotle in Adobo\n| 1 Large [[Onion]], peeled and sliced         \n| 1 whole [[Onion|onion]] peeled and cut in half\n| 45 ml of [[Corn oil|corn oil]]\n| 1 [[Garlic clove|garlic clove]], [[Minced|minced]]\n| 1 sprig of [[Marjoram|marjoram]]\n| 1 sprig of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 1 teaspoon of dry [[Mexican oregano|mexican oregano]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon of [[Cracked black pepper]]\n| \u00bd table spoon of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n====to serve====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n|16 small Corn Tostadas\n|Tender mix leaf salad\n|200 ml Cr\u00e8me Fraiche\n|100 g of Mexican crumble Queso Fresco\n|1 Avocado hass on slices\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| [[Roast]] the [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]] and 1 [[Onion|onion]] in half on a flat non-stick pan until everything is soft and the skin is blackened.\n| Place in a mortar or a [[Blender|blender]] and add La Coste\u00f1a Green Tomatillo and [[Chipotle in Adobo]].\n| [[Blend]] perfectly with the pestle or the [[Blender|blender]] until you obtain a thick [[Sauce|sauce]] and reserve.\n| Separately heat the [[Corn|corn]] in a [[Skillet|skillet]] and saut\u00e9 the [[Onion|onion]] slices stirring constantly until you get a golden colour. Add the [[Minced|minced]] [[Garlic|garlic]] and gently saut\u00e9 all together with the [[Marjoram|marjoram]], [[Thyme|thyme]] and [[Mexican oregano]].\n| Pour the mixture of [[Roasted tomatoes|roasted tomatoes]], La Coste\u00f1a Chipotle and [[tomatillos]] and medium [[Fry|fry]] for 10-15 minutes.\n| Season with [[Cracked black pepper|cracked black pepper]] and add half of the [[Salt|salt]]. Stir and check the flavour.\n| Place the [[tostadas]] on a plate and top with the beef Tinga stew.\n| Add [[Cr\u00e8me Fraiche]] to decorate. \n| Sprinkle with crumbled Mexican [[Queso Fresco]]\n| Garnish with the tender mixed salad leaves and a few [[avocado]] slices.\n}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:MexTrade.co.uk recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n===Recipe source===\n{{Template:RecipeCourtesyOfMexTrade.co.uk}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#onion #tostadas #crackedblackpepper #mexicanoregano #tingaderes #plumtomatoes #thyme #blender #beef #marjoram #garlicclove </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Edible tortilla baskets recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tortilla #tortillabaskets #spray #flourtortilla #wheat #brush #oliveoil #flour #yellowcornmeal #taco #miseenplace \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=These edible tortilla pots or baskets are easy to make and create fantastic edible bowls which enhances the appearance (and taste) of any meal\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 237\n|PortionCalories = 29\n|DatePublished=16th December 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Servings: 8 - 1 pack of soft tortillas makes 8 edible bowls\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  31 minutes\n|PrepTime =  25 minutes\n|CookTime =  6 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Tortilla baskets recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Genius!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Such a neat idea.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\nThese [[Tortilla pots|tortilla pots]], [[Tortilla|tortilla]] baskets are easy to prepare and make fantastic edible bowls which enhances the appearance (and taste) of any meal.\n\nThis cooking process works just as well with soft [[Flour|flour]] [[Wheat|wheat]] [[Flour tortilla|flour tortilla]] wraps as it does with soft [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wraps.\n\nThe idea is really simple, [[Spray|spray]] or [[Brush|brush]] the [[Tortilla|tortilla]], shape it into a greased bowl and back it in the [[Oven|oven]].  This hardens it  an turns it into a large crispy edible [[Taco|taco]]!\n\nYou must use an [[Oven|oven]]-proof bowl and you may have to experiment to find the bowl that produces the best shape.  I've found that  a small and a medium [[Glass|glass]] pyrex bowl work really well.\n\nFill them with the food of your choice, you'll find them to be much stronger than you might imagine.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 pack of soft [[Wheat|wheat]] [[Flour tortilla|flour tortilla]] wraps or soft [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]] [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wraps.\n| [[Olive oil]] for spraying for [[Brushing|brushing]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Lightly [[Spray|spray]] or [[Brush|brush]] your [[Oven|oven]]-proof bowls so the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wrap doesn't stick once it has been [[Baked|baked]].\n| Lightly [[Spray|spray]] the top surface of the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] with a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]], not too much.\n| Push the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] into your bowl so it makes a 'useful' shape.\n| [[Bake]] the [[Tortillas|tortillas]], in the bowls for 6 minutes or until they start to colour.\n| Watch them closely as the time between [[Browning|browning]] and burning is really short!\n| Carefully remove the bowls from the [[Oven|oven]] and invert them over [[Paper towels|paper towels]] and knock the shaped [[Tortilla|tortilla]] out onto the paper towels.\n| They remain soft and pliable while they are still hot so leave them upside down for 15 minutes or so to cool and harden, ready for use.\n| If like me, you don't have enough bowls, you can make these in batches, they keep pretty well for a day or so.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\n[[Image:Edible tortilla bowl.jpg.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Lightly greased and ready to bake]]\n</gallery>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortilla #tortillabaskets #spray #flourtortilla #wheat #brush #oliveoil #flour #yellowcornmeal #taco #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                ]

[[Lard]] could be used without any problems but the recipe would no longer be vegetarian.\n===Chef's note===\nIf you don't have a [[tortilla press]], use 2 chopping boards or just two sheets of wood as a substitute.  Place ball of [[dough]] between two non-stick surfaces such as small squares of [[Bake-O-Glide]] and stand on them!\n===Suppliers===\nSee the [[Tortilla Press]] page for UK suppliers.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]][[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortillapress #shortening #dough #griddle #fat #wheatflourtortillarecipe #masaharina #vegetableshortening #lard #hand #grilled </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Yellow rice (Mexican) Cooking with chillies recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#annattopowder #rice #onion #garlic #chillies #roastedredpeppers #vegetableoil #longgrainrice #chickenstock #achioteseeds #groundachioteseeds \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An unusual rice dish that uses ground achiote seeds (annatto powder) to colour it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 796\n|PortionCalories = 132\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 45 minutes \n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 35 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Yellow rice (Mexican) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Definitely Mexican</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Annatto makes this special!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Yellow rice (Mexican) ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Yellow rice - The ingredients]]\nAn unusual [[rice]] dish that uses ground [[achiote seeds]] ([[annatto powder]]) to colour it.  Although it's a Mexican dish, it would work in place of any rice dish.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 200g (7 oz) [[long grain rice]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[vegetable oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[ground achiote seeds]] ([[annatto powder]])\n| 1 small [[onion]], finely chopped\n| 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, crushed\n| 475 ml (16 fl oz) good [[vegetable stock|vegetable]] or [[chicken stock]]\n| 50 g (2 oz) pickled [[jalepeno chili slices]]\n| sea [[salt]]\n| Fresh [[coriander leaves]], chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a sieve, rinse the [[rice]] for a few minutes under cold running water  to remove excess starch.  The water should run clear once done\n| Heat the oil in a pan and fry the [[onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes until soft and translucent\n| Add the [[annatto powder]] and fry for a further 3 minutes\n| Mix the rice into the [[onion]] mix and stir well to coat all of the rice\n| Add the stock, bring to the boil and [[simmer]], covered, for 25 minutes or until the rice has absorbed all of the liquid.  A sheet or so of [[tin-foil]] under the pan lid helps to make a good seal\n| Add extra water if the [[rice]] dries out before it's cooked\n| Add the chopped [[chillies]] and add [[salt]] to taste\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe in a large bowl, garnished with [[coriander]] leaves\n\n===Variations===\n\nServe cold as a salad.\n\nIf you don't want to add [[chillies]], try some sliced [[roasted red peppers]] instead.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Rice]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#annattopowder #rice #onion #garlic #chillies #roastedredpeppers #vegetableoil #longgrainrice #chickenstock #achioteseeds #groundachioteseeds </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
